# <a name="microsoft-graph-permissions-reference"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ca75-104">Microsoft Graph 权限引用</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-104">Microsoft Graph permissions reference</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-105">若要使你的应用可访问 Microsoft Graph 中的数据，用户或管理员必须通过同意过程向其授予正确的权限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-105">For your app to access data in Microsoft Graph, the user or administrator must grant it the correct permissions via a consent process.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-106">本主题列出了与每个主要 Microsoft Graph API 集关联的权限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-106">This topic lists the permissions associated with each major set of Microsoft Graph APIs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-107">它还提供有关如何使用权限的指导。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-107">It also provides guidance about how to use the permissions.</span></span>

[!INCLUDE [auth-use-least-privileged](../includes/auth-use-least-privileged.md)]

<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-108">若要详细了解权限的工作原理，请参阅[身份验证和授权基础知识](auth/auth-concepts.md#microsoft-graph-permissions)，并观看以下视频。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-108">To learn more about how permissions work, see [Authentication and authorization basics](auth/auth-concepts.md#microsoft-graph-permissions), and watch the following video.</span></span>

> [!VIDEO https://www.youtube-nocookie.com/embed/yXYzgWWVdSM]

## <a name="microsoft-graph-permission-names"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ca75-109">Microsoft Graph 权限名称</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-109">Microsoft Graph permission names</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-p103">Microsoft Graph 权限名称遵循简单模式：_resource.operation.constraint_。例如，_User.Read_ 授予读取已登录用户的配置文件的权限，_User.ReadWrite_ 授予读取和修改已登录用户的配置文件的权限，而 _Mail.Send_ 则授予代表已登录用户发送邮件的权限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-p103">Microsoft Graph permission names follow a simple pattern: _resource.operation.constraint_. For example, _User.Read_ grants permission to read the profile of the signed-in user, _User.ReadWrite_ grants permission to read and modify the profile of the signed-in user, and _Mail.Send_ grants permission to send mail on behalf of the signed-in user.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-p104">名称的 _constraint_ 元素决定了你的应用程序在目录中具有的潜在访问范围。Microsoft Graph 当前支持以下约束：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-p104">The _constraint_ element of the name determines the potential extent of access your app will have within the directory. Currently Microsoft Graph supports the following constraints:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-p105">**All** 授予应用对目录中指定类型的所有资源执行操作的权限。例如，_User.Read.All_ 可能授予应用读取目录中所有用户的配置文件的特权。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-p105">**All** grants permission for the app to perform the operations on all of the resources of the specified type in a directory. For example, _User.Read.All_ potentially grants the app privileges to read the profiles of all of the users in a directory.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-p106">**Shared** 授予该应用对其他用户与已登录用户共享的资源执行操作的权限。此约束主要用于 Outlook 资源，如邮件、日历和联系人。例如，_Mail.Read.Shared_ 授予在已登录用户的邮箱中以及组织中的其他用户与已登录用户共享的邮箱中读取邮件的权限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-p106">**Shared** grants permission for the app to perform the operations on resources that other users have shared with the signed-in user. This constraint is mainly used with Outlook resources like mail, calendars, and contacts. For example, _Mail.Read.Shared_, grants privileges to read mail in the mailbox of the signed-in user as well as mail in mailboxes that other users in the organization have shared with the signed-in user.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-p107">**AppFolder** 授予应用在 OneDrive 专用文件夹中读取和写入文件的权限。此约束仅在 [文件权限](#files-permissions)上公开，并且仅适用于 Microsoft 帐户。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-p107">**AppFolder** grants permission for the app to read and write files in a dedicated folder in OneDrive. This constraint is only exposed on [Files permissions](#files-permissions) and is only valid for Microsoft accounts.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-p108">如果未指定 **任何约束**，则应用程序仅限于对已登录用户拥有的资源执行操作。例如，_User.Read_ 仅授予读取已登录用户的配置文件的特权，_Mail.Read_ 仅授予读取已登录用户邮箱中的邮件的权限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-p108">If **no constraint** is specified the app is limited to performing the operations on the resources owned by the signed-in user. For example, _User.Read_ grants privileges to read the profile of the signed-in user only, and _Mail.Read_ grants permission to read only mail in the mailbox of the signed-in user.</span></span>

> <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-123">**注意**：在委托场景中，授予应用的有效权限可能受到组织中已登录用户的特权的限制。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-123">**Note**: In delegated scenarios, the effective permissions granted to your app may be constrained by the privileges of the signed-in user in the organization.</span></span>

## <a name="microsoft-accounts-and-work-or-school-accounts"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ca75-124">Microsoft 帐户和工作或学校帐户</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-124">Microsoft accounts and work or school accounts</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-125">并非所有权限都适用于 Microsoft 帐户和工作或学校帐户。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-125">Not all permissions are valid for both Microsoft accounts and work or school accounts.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-126">你可以检查每个权限组的 **支持的 Microsoft 帐户** 列，以确定特定权限是否对 Microsoft 帐户和/或工作或学校帐户有效。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-126">You can check the **Microsoft Account Supported** column for each permission group to determine whether a specific permission is valid for Microsoft accounts, work or school accounts, or both.</span></span>

## <a name="permissions-availability-status"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ca75-127">权限可用性状态</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-127">Permissions availability status</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-128">[Azure 门户](https://portal.azure.com/)中的 Microsoft Graph 权限通常可用，并且处于 GA 状态，可供所有应用程序使用，除了少数处于预览或个人预览状态的集。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-128">Microsoft Graph permissions in the [Azure portal](https://portal.azure.com/) are generally available and in GA status for all apps to use, except for a few sets that are in preview or private preview status.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-129">预览中的权限对公众可用；它们可能会更改，并且可能无法升级到 GA 状态。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-129">Permissions in preview are available to the public; they may change and may not be promoted to GA status.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-130">个人预览状态中的权限不可用，并且永远不会对公众可用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-130">Permissions in private preview status are not and may never become available to the public.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-131">不要在生产应用中使用预览或个人预览状态中的权限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-131">Do not use permissions in preview or private preview status in production apps.</span></span>

## <a name="user-and-group-search-limitations-for-guest-users-in-organizations"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ca75-132">组织中来宾用户的用户和组搜索限制</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-132">User and group search limitations for guest users in organizations</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-133">用户和组搜索功能允许应用通过对 `/users` 或 `/groups` 资源集（例如 `https://graph.microsoft.com/v1.0/users`）执行查询来搜索组织目录中的任何用户或组。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-133">User and group search capabilities allow the app to search for any user or group in an organization's directory by performing queries against the `/users` or `/groups` resource set (for example, `https://graph.microsoft.com/v1.0/users`).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-134">管理员和用户都可以使用此功能；但来宾用户不可以。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-134">Both administrators and users have this capability; however, guest users do not.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-135">如果登录用户是来宾用户，应用程序可以读取特定用户或组的配置文件（例如，`https://graph.microsoft.com/v1.0/users/241f22af-f634-44c0-9a15-c8cd2cea5531`），具体视应用程序获得的授权而定；不过，不能对可能返回多个资源的 `/users` 或 `/groups` 资源集执行查询。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-135">If the signed-in user is a guest user, depending on the permissions an app has been granted, it can read the profile of a specific user or group (for example, `https://graph.microsoft.com/v1.0/users/241f22af-f634-44c0-9a15-c8cd2cea5531`); however, it cannot perform queries against the `/users` or `/groups` resource set that potentially return more than a single resource.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-136">借助授予的适当权限，应用程序可以读取用户或组的配置文件，具体是通过导航属性中的链接获取；例如，`/users/{id}/directReports` 或 `/groups/{id}/members`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-136">With the appropriate permissions, the app can read the profiles of users or groups that it obtains by following links in navigation properties; for example, `/users/{id}/directReports` or `/groups/{id}/members`.</span></span>

## <a name="limited-information-returned-for-inaccessible-member-objects"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ca75-137">为不可访问的成员对象返回有限的信息</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-137">Limited information returned for inaccessible member objects</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-138">容器对象（例如组）支持各种类型的成员（例如用户和设备）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-138">Container objects such as groups support members of various types, for example users and devices.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-139">当应用程序查询容器对象的成员身份，但无读取特定类型的权限时，将返回该类型的成员，但信息有限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-139">When an application queries the membership of a container object and does not have permission to read a certain type, members of that type are returned but with limited information.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-140">应用程序将收到 200 响应和一个对象集合。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-140">The application receives a 200 response and a collection of objects.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-141">对于应用程序有权读取的对象类型，返回完整信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-141">Complete information is returned for the object types that the application has permissions to read.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-142">对于应用程序没有读取权限的对象类型，仅返回对象类型和 ID。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-142">For the object types which the application does not have permission to read, only the the object type and ID are returned.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-143">这适用于 [directoryObject](/graph/api/resources/directoryobject) 类型的所有关系（而不仅仅是成员链接）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-143">This is applied to all relationships that are of [directoryObject](/graph/api/resources/directoryobject) type (not just member links).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-144">示例包括 `/groups/{id}/members`、`/users/{id}/memberOf` 或 `me/ownedObjects`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-144">Examples include `/groups/{id}/members`, `/users/{id}/memberOf` or `me/ownedObjects`.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-145">例如，假设一个应用程序具有 Microsoft Graph 的 [User.Read.All](#user-permissions) 和 [Group.Read.All](#group-permissions) 权限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-145">For example, let's say an application has [User.Read.All](#user-permissions) and [Group.Read.All](#group-permissions) permissions for Microsoft Graph.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-146">当前已创建一个组，且该组包含用户、组和设备。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-146">A group has been created and that group contains a user, a group, and a device.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-147">应用程序调用[列出组成员](/graph/api/group-list-members)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-147">The application calls [list group members](/graph/api/group-list-members).</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-148">应用程序可以访问组中的用户和组对象，而不能访问设备对象。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-148">The application has access to the user and group objects in the group, but not the device object.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-149">在响应中，将返回用户和组对象的所有选定属性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-149">In the response, all the selected properties of the user and group objects are returned.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-150">但是对于设备对象，仅返回有限的信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-150">For the device object, however, only limited information is returned.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-151">返回内容包括设备的数据类型和对象 ID，但所有其他属性的值均为 *null*。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-151">The data type and object ID are returned for the device, but all other properties have a value of *null*.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-152">没有权限的应用将不能使用 ID 获取实际对象。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-152">Apps without permission will not be able to use the ID to get the actual object.</span></span>

```http
GET https://graph.microsoft.com/v1.0/groups/{id}/members?$select=id,displayName,description,createdDateTime,deletedDateTime,homepage,loginUrl HTTP/1.1
```

<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-153">以下是 JSON 响应：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-153">The following is the JSON response:</span></span>

```json
{
"@odata.context":"https://graph.microsoft.com/v1.0/$metadata#directoryObjects(id,displayName,description,createdDateTime,deletedDateTime,homepage,loginUrl)",
    "value":[
        {
            "@odata.type":"#microsoft.graph.user",
            "id":"69d035a3-29c9-469f-809d-d21a4ae69e65",
            "displayName":"Jane Dane",
            "createdDateTime":"2019-09-18T09:06:51Z",
            "deletedDateTime":null
        },
        {
            "@odata.type":"#microsoft.graph.group",
            "id":"c43a7cc9-2d95-44b6-bf6a-6392e41949b4",
            "displayName":"Group 1",
            "description":null,
            "createdDateTime":"2019-10-24T01:34:35Z",
            "deletedDateTime":null
        },
        {
            "@odata.type":"#microsoft.graph.device",
            "id": "d282309e-f91d-43b6-badb-9e68aa4b4fc8",
            "accountEnabled":null,
            "deviceId":null,
            "displayName":null,
            "operatingSystem":null,
            "operatingSystemVersion":null
        }
    ]
}
```

## <a name="access-reviews-permissions"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ca75-154">访问评审权限</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-154">Access reviews permissions</span></span>

#### <a name="delegated-permissions"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ca75-155">委派权限</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-155">Delegated permissions</span></span>

|   <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-156">权限</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-156">Permission</span></span>    |  <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-157">显示字符串</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-157">Display String</span></span>   |  <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-158">说明</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-158">Description</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-159">需经过管理员同意</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-159">Admin Consent Required</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-160">支持的 Microsoft 帐户</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-160">Microsoft Account supported</span></span> |
|:----------------|:------------------|:-------------|:-----------------------|:--------------|
| <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-161">_AccessReview.Read.All_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-161">_AccessReview.Read.All_</span></span> |   <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-162">读取所有访问评审</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-162">Read all access reviews</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-163">允许应用代表已登录的用户读取访问评审。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-163">Allows the app to read access reviews on behalf of the signed-in user.</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-164">是</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-164">Yes</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-165">否</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-165">No</span></span> |
| <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-166">_AccessReview.ReadWrite.All_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-166">_AccessReview.ReadWrite.All_</span></span> |   <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-167">管理所有访问评审</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-167">Manage all access reviews</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-168">允许应用代表已登录的用户读取和写入访问评审。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-168">Allows the app to read and write access reviews on behalf of the signed-in user.</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-169">是</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-169">Yes</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-170">否</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-170">No</span></span> |
| <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-171">_AccessReview.ReadWrite.Membership_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-171">_AccessReview.ReadWrite.Membership_</span></span> |   <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-172">管理组和应用成员身份的访问评审</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-172">Manage access reviews for group and app memberships</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-173">允许应用代表已登录的用户读取和写入组和应用的访问评审。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-173">Allows the app to read and write access reviews of groups and apps on behalf of the signed-in user.</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-174">是</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-174">Yes</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-175">否</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-175">No</span></span> |



#### <a name="application-permissions"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ca75-176">应用程序权限</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-176">Application permissions</span></span>

|   <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-177">权限</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-177">Permission</span></span>    |  <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-178">显示字符串</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-178">Display String</span></span>   |  <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-179">说明</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-179">Description</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-180">需经过管理员同意</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-180">Admin Consent Required</span></span> |
|:-----------------------------|:-----------------------------------------|:-----------------|:-----------------|
| <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-181">_AccessReview.Read.All_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-181">_AccessReview.Read.All_</span></span> |   <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-182">读取所有访问评审</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-182">Read all access reviews</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-183">允许应用在没有登录的用户的情况下读取访问评审。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-183">Allows the app to read access reviews without a signed-in user.</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-184">是</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-184">Yes</span></span> |
| <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-185">_AccessReview.ReadWrite.Membership_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-185">_AccessReview.ReadWrite.Membership_</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-186">管理组和应用成员身份的访问评审</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-186">Manage access reviews for group and app memberships</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-187">允许应用在没有已登录用户的情况下管理组和应用的访问评审。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-187">Allows the app to manage access reviews of groups and apps without a signed-in user.</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-188">是</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-188">Yes</span></span> |


### <a name="remarks"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ca75-189">备注</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-189">Remarks</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-190">_AccessReview.Read.All_、_AccessReview.ReadWrite.All_、_AccessReview.ReadWrite.Membership_ 仅对于工作或学校帐户有效。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-190">_AccessReview.Read.All_, _AccessReview.ReadWrite.All_, _AccessReview.ReadWrite.Membership_ are valid only for work or school accounts.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-191">对于通过委派权限读取组或应用的访问评审的应用，登录的用户必须是以下管理员角色之一的成员：全局管理员、安全管理员、安全读取者或用户管理员。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-191">For an app with delegated permissions to read access reviews of a group or app, the signed-in user must be a member of one of the following administrator roles: Global Administrator, Security Administrator, Security Reader or User Administrator.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-192">对于通过委派权限读取组或应用的访问评审的应用，登录的用户必须是以下管理员角色之一的成员：全局管理员或用户管理员。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-192">For an app with delegated permissions to write access reviews of a group or app, the signed-in user must be a member of one of the following administrator roles: Global Administrator or User Administrator.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-193">对于通过委派权限读取 Azure AD 角色的访问评审的应用，登录的用户必须是以下管理员角色之一的成员：全局管理员、安全管理员、安全读取者或特权角色管理员。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-193">For an app with delegated permissions to read access reviews of an Azure AD role, the signed-in user must be a member of one of the following administrator roles: Global Administrator, Security Administrator, Security Reader or Privileged Role Administrator.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-194">对于通过委派权限写入 Azure AD 角色的访问评审的应用，登录的用户必须是以下管理员角色之一的成员：全局管理员或特权角色管理员。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-194">For an app with delegated permissions to write access reviews of an Azure AD role, the signed-in user must be a member of one of the following administrator roles: Global Administrator or Privileged Role Administrator.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-195">若要详细了解管理员角色，请参阅[在 Azure Active Directory 中分配管理员角色](/azure/active-directory/active-directory-assign-admin-roles)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-195">For more information about administrator roles, see [Assigning administrator roles in Azure Active Directory](/azure/active-directory/active-directory-assign-admin-roles).</span></span>

### <a name="remarks"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ca75-226">说明</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-226">Remarks</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-227">使用 _AdministrativeUnit.Read.All_ 权限，应用程序可以读取包括成员在内的管理单元信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-227">With the _AdministrativeUnit.Read.All_ permission an application can read administrative unit information including members.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-228">使用 _AdministrativeUnit.ReadWrite.All_ 权限，应用程序可以创建、读取、更新和删除包括成员在内的管理单元信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-228">With the _AdministrativeUnit.ReadWrite.All_ permission an application can create, read, update, and delete administrative unit information including members.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-229">_AdministrativeUnit.Read.All_ 和 _AdministrativeUnit.ReadWrite.All_ 仅对工作或学校帐户有效。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-229">_AdministrativeUnit.Read.All_ and _AdministrativeUnit.ReadWrite.All_ are valid only for work or school accounts.</span></span>

### <a name="example-usage"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ca75-230">用法示例</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-230">Example usage</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-231">_AdministrativeUnit.Read.All_：读取管理单元 (`GET /beta/administrativeUnits`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-231">_AdministrativeUnit.Read.All_: Read administrative units (`GET /beta/administrativeUnits`)</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-232">_AdministrativeUnit.Read.All_：读取管理单元成员列表 (`GET /beta/administrativeUnits/<id>/members`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-232">_AdministrativeUnit.Read.All_: Read members list of an administrative unit (`GET /beta/administrativeUnits/<id>/members`)</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-233">_AdministrativeUnit.ReadWrite.All_：创建管理单元 (`POST /beta/administrativeUnits`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-233">_AdministrativeUnit.ReadWrite.All_: Create an administrative unit (`POST /beta/administrativeUnits`)</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-234">_AdministrativeUnit.ReadWrite.All_：更新管理单元 (`PATCH /beta/administrativeUnits/<id>`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-234">_AdministrativeUnit.ReadWrite.All_: Update an administrative unit (`PATCH /beta/administrativeUnits/<id>`)</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-235">_AdministrativeUnit.ReadWrite.All_：将成员添加到管理单元 (`POST /beta/administrativeUnits/<id>/members`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-235">_AdministrativeUnit.ReadWrite.All_: Add members to an administrative unit  (`POST /beta/administrativeUnits/<id>/members`)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-236">有关涉及多个权限的更复杂的情况，请参阅[权限方案](#permission-scenarios)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-236">For more complex scenarios involving multiple permissions, see [Permission scenarios](#permission-scenarios).</span></span>

### <a name="remarks"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ca75-279">注解</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-279">Remarks</span></span>

### <a name="example-usage"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ca75-281">用法示例</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-281">Example usage</span></span>

#### <a name="delegated"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ca75-282">委派</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-282">Delegated</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-283">_AppCatalog.ReadWrite.All_：[：列出目录中的所有应用程序](/graph/api/teamsapp-list?view=graph-rest-beta&preserve-view=true) (`GET /beta/appCatalogs/teamsApps`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-283">_AppCatalog.ReadWrite.All_: [List all applications in catalog](/graph/api/teamsapp-list?view=graph-rest-beta&preserve-view=true) (`GET /beta/appCatalogs/teamsApps`)</span></span>

### <a name="remarks"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ca75-331">备注</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-331">Remarks</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-332">_Application.ReadWrite.OwnedBy_ 权限允许与 _Application.ReadWrite.All_ 相同的操作，只不过前者只允许对调用应用充当所有者的应用程序和服务主体执行这些操作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-332">The _Application.ReadWrite.OwnedBy_ permission allows the same operations as _Application.ReadWrite.All_ except that the former allows these operations only on applications and service principals that the calling app is an owner of.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-333">所有权由目标 [application](/graph/api/application-list-owners?view=graph-rest-beta&preserve-view=true) 或 [service principal](/graph/api/serviceprincipal-list-owners?view=graph-rest-beta&preserve-view=true) 资源上的 `owners` 导航属性指示。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-333">Ownership is indicated by the `owners` navigation property on the target [application](/graph/api/application-list-owners?view=graph-rest-beta&preserve-view=true) or [service principal](/graph/api/serviceprincipal-list-owners?view=graph-rest-beta&preserve-view=true) resource.</span></span>
> <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-334">注意：使用 _Application.Read Write.Owned by_ 权限调用 `GET /applications` 以列出应用程序将失败，并显示 403。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-334">NOTE: Using the _Application.ReadWrite.OwnedBy_ permission to call `GET /applications` to list applications will fail with a 403.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-335">请改为使用 `GET servicePrincipals/{id}/ownedObjects` 列出调用应用程序充当所有者的应用程序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-335">Instead use `GET servicePrincipals/{id}/ownedObjects` to list the applications owned by the calling application.</span></span>

### <a name="example-usage"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ca75-336">用法示例</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-336">Example usage</span></span>

#### <a name="delegated"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ca75-337">委派</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-337">Delegated</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-338">_Application.Read.All_：列出所有应用程序 (`GET /beta/applications`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-338">_Application.Read.All_: List all applications (`GET /beta/applications`)</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-339">_Application.ReadWrite.All_：更新服务主体 (`PATCH /beta/servicePrincipals/{id}`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-339">_Application.ReadWrite.All_: Update a service principal (`PATCH /beta/servicePrincipals/{id}`)</span></span>

#### <a name="application"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ca75-340">应用程序</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-340">Application</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-341">_Application.Read.All_：列出所有应用程序 (`GET /beta/applications`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-341">_Application.Read.All_: List all applications (`GET /beta/applications`)</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-342">_Application.ReadWrite.All_：删除服务主体 (`DELETE /beta/servicePrincipals/{id}`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-342">_Application.ReadWrite.All_: Delete a service principal (`DELETE /beta/servicePrincipals/{id}`)</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-343">_Application.ReadWrite.OwnedBy_：创建应用程序 (`POST /beta/applications`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-343">_Application.ReadWrite.OwnedBy_: Create an application (`POST /beta/applications`)</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-344">_Application.ReadWrite.OwnedBy_：列出调用应用程序拥有的所有应用程序 (`GET /beta/servicePrincipals/{id}/ownedObjects`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-344">_Application.ReadWrite.OwnedBy_: List all applications owned by the calling application (`GET /beta/servicePrincipals/{id}/ownedObjects`)</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-345">_Application.ReadWrite.OwnedBy_：向拥有的应用程序添加另一个所有者 (`POST /applications/{id}/owners/$ref`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-345">_Application.ReadWrite.OwnedBy_: Add another owner to an owned application (`POST /applications/{id}/owners/$ref`).</span></span>
    > <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-346">注意：这可能需要其他权限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-346">NOTE: This may require additional permissions.</span></span>

### <a name="example-usage"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ca75-478">用法示例</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-478">Example usage</span></span>

#### <a name="delegated"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ca75-479">委派</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-479">Delegated</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-480">_Calendars.Read_：获取从 2017 年 4 月 23 日到 2017 年 4 月 29 日用户日历中的事件 (`GET /me/calendarView?startDateTime=2017-04-23T00:00:00&endDateTime=2017-04-29T00:00:00`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-480">_Calendars.Read_: Get events on the user's calendar between April 23, 2017 and April 29, 2017 (`GET /me/calendarView?startDateTime=2017-04-23T00:00:00&endDateTime=2017-04-29T00:00:00`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-481">_Calendars.Read.Shared_：查找所有与会者都均有空参加的会议时间 (`POST /users/{id|userPrincipalName}/findMeetingTimes`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-481">_Calendars.Read.Shared_: Find meeting times where all attendees are available (`POST /users/{id|userPrincipalName}/findMeetingTimes`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-482">_Calendars.ReadWrite_：将事件添加到用户日历 (`POST /me/events`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-482">_Calendars.ReadWrite_: Add an event to the user's calendar (`POST /me/events`).</span></span>

#### <a name="application"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ca75-483">应用程序</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-483">Application</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-484">_Calendars.Read_：在 bob@contoso.com 组织整理的会议室日历中查找事件 (`GET /users/{id | userPrincipalName}/events?$filter=organizer/emailAddress/address eq 'bob@contoso.com'`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-484">_Calendars.Read_: Find events in a conference room's calendar organized by bob@contoso.com (`GET /users/{id | userPrincipalName}/events?$filter=organizer/emailAddress/address eq 'bob@contoso.com'`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-485">_Calendars.Read_：列出 5 月份用户日历上的所有事件 (`GET /users/{id | userPrincipalName}/calendarView?startDateTime=2017-05-01T00:00:00&endDateTime=2017-06-01T00:00:00`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-485">_Calendars.Read_: List all events on a user's calendar for the month of May (`GET /users/{id | userPrincipalName}/calendarView?startDateTime=2017-05-01T00:00:00&endDateTime=2017-06-01T00:00:00`)</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-486">_Calendars.ReadWrite_：将获准休假事件添加到用户日历 (`POST /users/{id | userPrincipalName}/events`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-486">_Calendars.ReadWrite_: Add an event to a user's calendar for approved time off  (`POST /users/{id | userPrincipalName}/events`).</span></span>

### <a name="example-usage"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ca75-521">用法示例</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-521">Example usage</span></span>

#### <a name="application"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ca75-522">应用程序</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-522">Application</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-523">_Calls.Initiate.All_：从应用程序向组织中的某个用户发起对等通话 (`POST /beta/communications/calls`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-523">_Calls.Initiate.All_: Make a peer-to-peer call from the application to a user in the organization (`POST /beta/communications/calls`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-524">_Calls.InitiateGroupCall.All_：从应用程序向组织中的一组用户发起组通话 (`POST /beta/communications/calls`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-524">_Calls.InitiateGroupCall.All_: Make a group call from the application to a group of users in the organization (`POST /beta/communications/calls`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-525">_Calls.JoinGroupCall.All_：从应用程序加入组通话或联机会议 (`POST /beta/communications/calls`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-525">_Calls.JoinGroupCall.All_: Join a group call or online meeting from the application (`POST /beta/communications/calls`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-526">_Calls.JoinGroupCallasGuest.All_：从应用程序加入组通话或联机会议，但应用程序在会议中仅具有来宾特权 (`POST /beta/communications/calls`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-526">_Calls.JoinGroupCallasGuest.All_: Join a group call or online meeting from the application, but the application only has guest privileges in the meeting (`POST /beta/communications/calls`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-527">_Calls.AccessMedia.All_：创建或加入某个通话，且应用将能够直接访问该通话中的参与者媒体数据流 (`POST /beta/communications/calls`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-527">_Calls.AccessMedia.All_: Create or join a call and the app gets direct access to participant media streams in the call (`POST /beta/communications/calls`).</span></span>

> <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-528">**注意：** 有关请求示例，请参阅 [创建通话](/graph/api/application-post-calls?view=graph-rest-beta&preserve-view=true)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-528">**Note:** For request examples, see [Create call](/graph/api/application-post-calls?view=graph-rest-beta&preserve-view=true).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-529">有关涉及多个权限的更复杂的情况，请参阅[权限方案](#permission-scenarios)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-529">For more complex scenarios involving multiple permissions, see [Permission scenarios](#permission-scenarios).</span></span>

|<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-534">权限</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-534">Permission</span></span>    |<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-535">显示字符串</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-535">Display String</span></span>   |<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-536">说明</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-536">Description</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-537">需经过管理员同意</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-537">Admin Consent Required</span></span> |

### <a name="remarks"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ca75-542">备注</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-542">Remarks</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-543">_CallRecords.Read.All_ 权限为组织内每次通话和联机会议（包括与外部电话号码的通话）授权 [callRecords](/graph/api/resources/callrecords-callrecord) 的特权访问。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-543">The _CallRecords.Read.All_ permission grants an application privileged access to [callRecords](/graph/api/resources/callrecords-callrecord) for every call and online meeting within your organization, including calls to and from external phone numbers.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-544">这包括与参与呼叫的人员有关的潜在敏感详细信息，以及与这些通话和会议相关的、可用于网络疑难解答的技术信息（IP地址、设备详细信息和其他网络信息）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-544">This includes potentially sensitive details about who participated in the call, as well as technical information pertaining to these calls and meetings that can be used for network troubleshooting, such as IP addresses, device details, and other network information.</span></span>

> <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-545">**重要说明：** 应谨慎为应用程序授予这些权限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-545">**Important:** Discretion should be used when granting these permissions to applications.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-546">通话记录可提供业务运营的见解，因此可能成为恶意参与者的目标。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-546">Call records can provide insights into the operation of your business, and so can be a target for malicious actors.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-547">仅为你信任的应用程序授予这些权限，以满足你的数据保护要求。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-547">Only grant these permissions to applications you trust to meet your data protection requirements.</span></span>

> <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-548">**重要说明：** 请确保你遵守有关通信的数据保护和机密性方面的法律和法规。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-548">**Important:** Make sure that you are compliant with the laws and regulations in your area regarding data protection and confidentiality of communications.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-549">有关详细信息，请参阅[使用条款](/legal/microsoft-apis/terms-of-use)并咨询法律顾问。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-549">Please see the [Terms of Use](/legal/microsoft-apis/terms-of-use) and consult with your legal counsel for more information.</span></span>

<br/>

### <a name="example-usage"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ca75-550">用法示例</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-550">Example usage</span></span>

#### <a name="application"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ca75-551">应用程序</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-551">Application</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-552">_CallRecords.Read.All_：检索通话记录 (`GET /v1.0/communications/callRecords/{id}`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-552">_CallRecords.Read.All_: Retrieve a call record (`GET /v1.0/communications/callRecords/{id}`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-553">_CallRecords.Read.All_：订阅新的通话记录 (`POST /v1.0/subscriptions`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-553">_CallRecords.Read.All_: Subscribe to new call records (`POST /v1.0/subscriptions`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-554">_CallRecords.Read.All_：检索指定时间范围 (`GET /v1.0/communications/callRecords/microsoft.graph.callRecords.getDirectRoutingCalls(fromDateTime={start date and time),toDateTime={end date and time))`) 内的直接路由通话记录。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-554">_CallRecords.Read.All_: Retrieve direct routing call records within the specified time range (`GET /v1.0/communications/callRecords/microsoft.graph.callRecords.getDirectRoutingCalls(fromDateTime={start date and time),toDateTime={end date and time))`)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-555">有关涉及多个权限的更复杂的情况，请参阅[权限方案](#permission-scenarios)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-555">For more complex scenarios involving multiple permissions, see [Permission scenarios](#permission-scenarios).</span></span>

### <a name="example-usage"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ca75-867">用法示例</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-867">Example usage</span></span>

#### <a name="delegated"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ca75-868">委派</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-868">Delegated</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-869">_CloudPC.Read.All_：查看所有云电脑（`GET /deviceManagement/virtualEndpoint/cloudPCs`）的属性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-869">_CloudPC.Read.All_: View the properties of all Cloud PCs (`GET /deviceManagement/virtualEndpoint/cloudPCs`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-870">_CloudPC.ReadWrite.All_：编辑云电脑设置策略（`PATCH /deviceManagement/virtualEndpoint/provisioningPolicies/{id}`）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-870">_CloudPC.ReadWrite.All_: Edit the Cloud PC provisioning policy (`PATCH /deviceManagement/virtualEndpoint/provisioningPolicies/{id}`).</span></span>

#### <a name="application"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ca75-871">应用程序</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-871">Application</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-872">_CloudPC.Read.All_：查看所有云电脑（`GET /deviceManagement/virtualEndpoint/cloudPCs`）的属性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-872">_CloudPC.Read.All_: View the properties of all Cloud PCs (`GET /deviceManagement/virtualEndpoint/cloudPCs`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-873">_CloudPC.ReadWrite.All_：编辑云电脑设置策略（`PATCH /deviceManagement/virtualEndpoint/provisioningPolicies/{id}`）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-873">_CloudPC.ReadWrite.All_: Edit the Cloud PC provisioning policy (`PATCH /deviceManagement/virtualEndpoint/provisioningPolicies/{id}`).</span></span>

|<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-916">_Contacts.Read.Shared_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-916">_Contacts.Read.Shared_</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-917">读取用户联系人和共享联系人</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-917">Read user and shared contacts</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-918">允许应用读取用户有权访问的联系人，包括用户个人联系人和共享联系人。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-918">Allows the app to read contacts that the user has permissions to access, including the user's own and shared contacts.</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-919">否</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-919">No</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-920">否</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-920">No</span></span>|
|<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-921">_Contacts.ReadWrite_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-921">_Contacts.ReadWrite_</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-922">具有对用户联系人的完整访问权限</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-922">Have full access to user contacts</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-923">允许应用创建、读取、更新和删除用户联系人。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-923">Allows the app to create, read, update, and delete user contacts.</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-924">否</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-924">No</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-925">是</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-925">Yes</span></span>|

#### <a name="application-permissions"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ca75-931">应用程序权限</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-931">Application permissions</span></span>

|<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-932">权限</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-932">Permission</span></span>    |<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-933">显示字符串</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-933">Display String</span></span>   |<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-934">说明</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-934">Description</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-935">需经过管理员同意</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-935">Admin Consent Required</span></span> |
|:-----------------------------|:-----------------------------------------|:-----------------|:-----------------|
|<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-936">_Contacts.Read_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-936">_Contacts.Read_</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-937">读取所有邮箱中的联系人</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-937">Read contacts in all mailboxes</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-938">允许应用在没有已登录用户的情况下读取所有邮箱中的所有联系人。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-938">Allows the app to read all contacts in all mailboxes without a signed-in user.</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-939">是</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-939">Yes</span></span> |
|<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-940">_Contacts.ReadWrite_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-940">_Contacts.ReadWrite_</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-941">读取和写入所有邮箱中的联系人</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-941">Read and write contacts in all mailboxes</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-942">允许应用在没有登录用户的情况下创建、读取、更新和删除所有邮箱中的全部联系人。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-942">Allows the app to create, read, update, and delete all contacts in all mailboxes without a signed-in user.</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-943">是</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-943">Yes</span></span> |

> <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-944">**重要说明** 管理员可以配置 [应用程序访问策略](auth-limit-mailbox-access.md)，以限制应用程序访问 _特定_ 邮箱，而不是组织中的所有邮箱，即使该应用程序已被授予 Contacts.Read 或 Contacts.ReadWrite 的应用程序权限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-944">**Important** Administrators can configure [application access policy](auth-limit-mailbox-access.md) to limit app access to _specific_ mailboxes and not all the mailboxes in the organization, even if the app has been granted the application permissions of Contacts.Read or Contacts.ReadWrite.</span></span>

### <a name="example-usage"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ca75-945">用法示例</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-945">Example usage</span></span>
#### <a name="delegated"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ca75-946">委派</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-946">Delegated</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-947">_Contacts.Read_：从登录用户的一个顶层联系人文件夹读取联系人 (`GET /me/contactfolders/{Id}/contacts/{id}`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-947">_Contacts.Read_: Read a contact from one of the top-level contact folders of the signed-in user (`GET /me/contactfolders/{Id}/contacts/{id}`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-948">_Contacts.ReadWrite_：更新登录用户的一个联系人的联系人照片 (`PUT /me/contactfolders/{contactFolderId}/contacts/{id}/photo/$value`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-948">_Contacts.ReadWrite_: Update the contact photo of one of the signed-in user's contacts (`PUT /me/contactfolders/{contactFolderId}/contacts/{id}/photo/$value`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-949">_Contacts.ReadWrite_：将联系人添加到登录用户的根文件夹 (`POST /me/contacts`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-949">_Contacts.ReadWrite_: Add contacts to the root folder of the signed-in user (`POST /me/contacts`).</span></span>

#### <a name="application"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ca75-950">应用程序</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-950">Application</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-951">_Contacts.Read_：从组织中任意用户的一个顶层联系人文件夹读取联系人 (`GET /users/{id | userPrincipalName}/contactfolders/{Id}/contacts/{id}`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-951">_Contacts.Read_: Read contacts from one of the top-level contact folders of any user in the organization (`GET /users/{id | userPrincipalName}/contactfolders/{Id}/contacts/{id}`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-952">_Contacts.ReadWrite_：更新组织中任意用户的所有联系人的照片 (`PUT /users/{id | userPrincipalName}/contactfolders/{contactFolderId}/contacts/{id}/photo/$value`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-952">_Contacts.ReadWrite_: Update the photo for any contact of any user in an organization (`PUT /users/{id | userPrincipalName}/contactfolders/{contactFolderId}/contacts/{id}/photo/$value`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-953">_Contacts.ReadWrite_：将联系人添加到组织中任意用户的根文件夹 (`POST /users/{id | userPrincipalName}/contacts`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-953">_Contacts.ReadWrite_: Add contacts to the root folder of any user in the organization (`POST /users/{id | userPrincipalName}/contacts`).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-954">有关涉及多个权限的更复杂的情况，请参阅[权限方案](#permission-scenarios)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-954">For more complex scenarios involving multiple permissions, see [Permission scenarios](#permission-scenarios).</span></span>

Does not allow device creation, device deletion, or update of device alternative security identifiers.</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-990">是</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-990">Yes</span></span> |

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-991">2020 年 12 月 3 日之前，当应用程序权限 *Device.Read.All* 被授予时，[设备管理员](/azure/active-directory/users-groups-roles/directory-assign-admin-roles#deprecated-roles)目录角色也被分配给了应用程序的服务主体。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-991">Before December 3rd, 2020, when the application permission *Device.ReadWrite.All* was granted, the [Device Managers](/azure/active-directory/users-groups-roles/directory-assign-admin-roles#deprecated-roles) directory role was also assigned to the app's service principal.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-992">撤销关联的应用程序权限后，不会自动删除此目录角色分配。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-992">This directory role assignment is not removed automatically when the associated application permissions is revoked.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-993">为确保删除应用程序对设备的读写权限，客户还必须删除授予该应用程序的所有相关目录角色。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-993">To ensure that an application's access to read or write to devices is removed, customers must also remove any related directory roles that were granted to the application.</span></span>
> 
> <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-994">禁用此行为的服务更新于 2020 年 12 月 3 日开始推出。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-994">A service update disabling this behavior began rolling out on December 3rd, 2020.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-995">部署到所有客户，2021 年 1 月 11 日完成。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-995">Deployment to all customers completed on January 11th, 2021.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-996">授予应用程序权限后，系统不再自动分配目录角色。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-996">Directory roles are no longer automatically assigned when application permissions are granted.</span></span>

### <a name="example-usage"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ca75-997">用法示例</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-997">Example usage</span></span>

#### <a name="application"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ca75-998">应用程序</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-998">Application</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-999">_Device.ReadWrite.All_：读取组织中的所有已注册设备 (`GET /devices`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-999">_Device.ReadWrite.All_: Read all registered devices in the organization (`GET /devices`).</span></span>

## <a name="directory-permissions"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1001">目录权限</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1001">Directory permissions</span></span>

#### <a name="delegated-permissions"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1002">委派权限</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1002">Delegated permissions</span></span>

|   <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1003">权限</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1003">Permission</span></span>    |  <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1004">显示字符串</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1004">Display String</span></span>   |  <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1005">说明</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1005">Description</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1006">需经过管理员同意</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1006">Admin Consent Required</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1007">支持的 Microsoft 帐户</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1007">Microsoft Account supported</span></span> |
|:----------------|:------------------|:-------------|:-----------------------|:--------------|
| <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1008">_Directory.Read.All_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1008">_Directory.Read.All_</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1009">读取目录数据</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1009">Read directory data</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1010">允许应用程序读取组织目录中的数据，如用户、组和应用程序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1010">Allows the app to read data in your organization's directory, such as users, groups and apps.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1011">**注意**：如果应用程序已在自己组织的租户中注册，用户可能会同意应用程序要求必须有此权限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1011">**Note**: Users may consent to applications that require this permission if the application is registered in their own organization’s tenant.</span></span>| <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1012">是</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1012">Yes</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1013">否</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1013">No</span></span> |
| <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1014">_Directory.ReadWrite.All_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1014">_Directory.ReadWrite.All_</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1015">读取和写入目录数据</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1015">Read and write directory data</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-p141">允许应用读取和写入组织目录中的数据，如用户和组。它不允许应用删除用户或组，或重置用户密码。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-p141">Allows the app to read and write data in your organization's directory, such as users, and groups. It does not allow the app to delete users or groups, or reset user passwords.</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1018">是</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1018">Yes</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1019">否</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1019">No</span></span> |
| <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1020">_Directory.AccessAsUser.All_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1020">_Directory.AccessAsUser.All_</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1021">以登录用户身份访问目录</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1021">Access directory as the signed-in user</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1022">允许应用以登录用户身份访问目录中的信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1022">Allows the app to have the same access to information in the directory as the signed-in user.</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1023">是</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1023">Yes</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1024">否</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1024">No</span></span> |

#### <a name="application-permissions"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1025">应用程序权限</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1025">Application permissions</span></span>

### <a name="remarks"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1039">注解</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1039">Remarks</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1040">Directory 权限提供访问目录资源（如组织中的 [user](/graph/api/resources/user)、[group](/graph/api/resources/group) 和 [device](/graph/api/resources/device)）的最高级特权。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1040">Directory permissions provide the highest level of privilege for accessing directory resources such as [user](/graph/api/resources/user), [group](/graph/api/resources/group), and [device](/graph/api/resources/device) in an organization.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1041">它们还专门控制对其他目录资源的访问，如 [组织联系人](/graph/api/resources/orgcontact?view=graph-rest-beta&preserve-view=true)、[架构扩展 API](/graph/api/resources/schemaextension?view=graph-rest-beta&preserve-view=true)、[Privileged Identity Management (PIM) API](/graph/api/resources/privilegedidentitymanagement-root?view=graph-rest-beta&preserve-view=true)，以及 v1.0 和 beta API 参考文档中 **Azure Active Directory** 节点下列出的许多资源和 API。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1041">They also exclusively control access to other directory resources like: [organizational contacts](/graph/api/resources/orgcontact?view=graph-rest-beta&preserve-view=true), [schema extension APIs](/graph/api/resources/schemaextension?view=graph-rest-beta&preserve-view=true), [Privileged Identity Management (PIM) APIs](/graph/api/resources/privilegedidentitymanagement-root?view=graph-rest-beta&preserve-view=true), as well as many of the resources and APIs listed under the **Azure Active Directory** node in the v1.0 and beta API reference documentation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1042">其中包括管理单元、目录角色、目录设置、策略等。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1042">These include administrative units, directory roles, directory settings, policy, and many more.</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1043">2020 年 12 月 3 日之前，当向应用程序授予权限 *Directory.Read.All* 时， [目录阅读器](/azure/active-directory/users-groups-roles/directory-assign-admin-roles#directory-readers-permissions) 目录角色也分配给了应用程序的服务主体。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1043">Before December 3rd, 2020, when the application permission *Directory.Read.All* was granted, the [Directory Readers](/azure/active-directory/users-groups-roles/directory-assign-admin-roles#directory-readers-permissions) directory role was also assigned to the app's service principal.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1044">当 *Directory.ReadWrite.* 授予所有项目时， [作者](/azure/active-directory/users-groups-roles/directory-assign-admin-roles#directory-writers-permissions) 分配了目录角色。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1044">When *Directory.ReadWrite.All* was granted, the [Directory Writers](/azure/active-directory/users-groups-roles/directory-assign-admin-roles#directory-writers-permissions) directory role was also assigned.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1045">撤销关联的应用程序权限时，不会自动删除这些目录角色。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1045">These directory roles are not removed automatically when the associated application permissions are revoked.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1046">要删除应用程序对目录的读写权限，客户还必须删除授予该应用程序的所有目录角色。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1046">To remove an application's access to read or write to the directory, customers must also remove any directory roles that were granted to the application.</span></span>
> 
> <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1047">禁用此行为的服务更新于 2020 年 12 月 3 日开始推出。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1047">A service update disabling this behavior began rolling out on December 3rd, 2020.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1048">部署到所有客户，2021 年 1 月 11 日完成。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1048">Deployment to all customers completed on January 11th, 2021.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1049">授予应用程序权限后，系统不再自动分配目录角色。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1049">Directory roles are no longer automatically assigned when application permissions are granted.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1050">_Directory.ReadWrite.All_ 权限可授予以下特权：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1050">The _Directory.ReadWrite.All_ permission grants the following privileges:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1051">完全读取所有目录资源（包括声明属性和导航属性）</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1051">Full read of all directory resources (both declared properties and navigation properties)</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1052">创建和更新用户</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1052">Create and update users</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1053">禁用和启用用户（而不是公司管理员）</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1053">Disable and enable users (but not Company Administrator)</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1054">设置用户可选安全 ID（而不是管理员）</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1054">Set user alternative security ID (but not administrators)</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1055">创建和更新组</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1055">Create and update groups</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1056">管理组成员</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1056">Manage group memberships</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1057">更新组所有者</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1057">Update group owner</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1058">管理许可证分配</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1058">Manage license assignments</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1059">在应用程序上定义架构扩展</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1059">Define schema extensions on applications</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1060">管理目录设置</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1060">Manage directory settings</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1061">管理管理员许可工作流配置（但不要求管理员许可或授权授予管理员许可的用户）</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1061">Manage admin consent workflow configuration (but not whether admin consent is required or who is authorized to grant admin consent)</span></span>

> <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1062">**注意**：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1062">**Note**:</span></span>
> - <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1063">无权重置用户密码。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1063">No rights to reset user passwords.</span></span>
> - <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1064">如需更新其他用户的 **businessPhones**、**mobilePhone** 或 **otherMails** 属性，仅允许针对非管理员或分配了以下角色之一的用户执行该操作：目录读取者、来宾邀请者、消息中心读取者和报告读取者。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1064">Updating another user's **businessPhones**, **mobilePhone**, or **otherMails** property is only allowed on users who are non-administrators or assigned one of the following roles: Directory Readers, Guest Inviter, Message Center Reader and Reports Reader.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1065">有关详细信息，请参阅 [Azure AD 可用角色](/azure/active-directory/users-groups-roles/directory-assign-admin-roles#available-roles)中的支持人员（密码）管理员。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1065">For more details, see Helpdesk (Password) Administrator in [Azure AD available roles](/azure/active-directory/users-groups-roles/directory-assign-admin-roles#available-roles).</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1066">这适用于获得了 User.ReadWrite.All 或 Directory.ReadWrite.All 委派或应用程序权限的应用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1066">This is the case for apps granted either the User.ReadWrite.All or Directory.ReadWrite.All delegated or application permissions.</span></span>
> - <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1067">无权删除资源（包括用户或组）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1067">No rights to delete resources (including users or groups).</span></span>
> - <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-p147">具体排除上面未列出的资源的创建或更新。 这包括：应用程序，oAauth2Permissiongrant，appRoleAssignment，设备，servicePrincipal，组织，域等。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-p147">Specifically excludes create or update for resources not listed above. This includes: application, oAauth2Permissiongrant, appRoleAssignment, device, servicePrincipal, organization, domains, and so on.</span></span>


### <a name="example-usage"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1070">用法示例</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1070">Example usage</span></span>

#### <a name="delegated"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1071">委派</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1071">Delegated</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1072">_Directory.Read.All_：列出组织中的所有管理单元 (`GET /beta/administrativeUnits`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1072">_Directory.Read.All_: List all administrative units in an organization (`GET /beta/administrativeUnits`)</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1073">_Directory.ReadWrite.All_：将成员添加到目录角色 (`POST /directoryRoles/{id}/members/$ref`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1073">_Directory.ReadWrite.All_: Add members to a directory role (`POST /directoryRoles/{id}/members/$ref`)</span></span>

#### <a name="application"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1074">应用程序</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1074">Application</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1075">_Directory.Read.All_：列出用户的所有成员资格，包括目录角色和管理单元 (`GET /beta/users/{id}/memberOf`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1075">_Directory.Read.All_: List all memberships of a user, including directory roles and administrative units (`GET /beta/users/{id}/memberOf`)</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1076">_Directory.Read.All_：列出所有组成员，包括服务主体 (`GET /beta/groups/{id}/members`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1076">_Directory.Read.All_: List all group members, including service principals (`GET /beta/groups/{id}/members`)</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1077">_Directory.ReadWrite.All_：向组添加所有者 (`POST /groups/{id}/owners/$ref`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1077">_Directory.ReadWrite.All_: Add an owner to a group (`POST /groups/{id}/owners/$ref`)</span></span>


<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1078">有关涉及多个权限的更复杂的情况，请参阅[权限方案](#permission-scenarios)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1078">For more complex scenarios involving multiple permissions, see [Permission scenarios](#permission-scenarios).</span></span>

### <a name="example-usage"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1205">用法示例</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1205">Example usage</span></span>

#### <a name="delegated"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1206">委派</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1206">Delegated</span></span>

### <a name="remarks"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1297">注解</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1297">Remarks</span></span>

> <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1298">**注意**：对于个人帐户，Files.Read 和 Files.ReadWrite 还会授予与登录用户共享的文件的访问权限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1298">**Note**: For personal accounts, Files.Read and Files.ReadWrite also grant access to files shared with the signed-in user.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-p151">Files.Read.Selected 和 Files.ReadWrite.Selected 委派权限仅在工作或学校帐户上有效，并仅在处理 [Office 365 文件处理程序 (v1.0)](/previous-versions/office/office-365-api/) 时才公开。它们不应该用来直接调用 Microsoft Graph API。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-p151">The Files.Read.Selected and Files.ReadWrite.Selected delegated permissions are only valid on work or school accounts and are only exposed for working with [Office 365 file handlers (v1.0)](/previous-versions/office/office-365-api/). They should not be used for directly calling Microsoft Graph APIs.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1301">Files.ReadWrite.AppFolder 委派权限仅适于个人帐户，并仅用于访问带有 OneDrive [获取特殊文件夹](/graph/api/drive-get-specialfolder) Microsoft Graph API 的[应用程序根特殊文件夹](https://dev.onedrive.com/misc/appfolder.htm)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1301">The Files.ReadWrite.AppFolder delegated permission is only valid for personal accounts and is used for accessing the [App Root special folder](https://dev.onedrive.com/misc/appfolder.htm) with the OneDrive [Get special folder](/graph/api/drive-get-specialfolder) Microsoft Graph API.</span></span>


### <a name="example-usage"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1302">用法示例</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1302">Example usage</span></span>

#### <a name="delegated"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1303">委派</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1303">Delegated</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1304">_Files.Read_：读取登录用户的 OneDrive 中存储的文件 (`GET /me/drive/root/children`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1304">_Files.Read_: Read files stored in the signed-in user's OneDrive (`GET /me/drive/root/children`)</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1305">_Files.Read.All_：列出与登录用户共享的文件 (`GET /me/drive/root/sharedWithMe`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1305">_Files.Read.All_: Read files shared with the signed-in user (`GET /me/drive/root/sharedWithMe`)</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1306">_Files.ReadWrite_：在登录用户的 OneDrive 中写入文件 (`PUT /me/drive/root/children/filename.txt/content`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1306">_Files.ReadWrite_: Write a file in the signed-in user's OneDrive (`PUT /me/drive/root/children/filename.txt/content`)</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1307">_Files.ReadWrite.All_：写入与用户共享的文件 (`PUT /users/rgregg@contoso.com/drive/root/children/file.txt/content`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1307">_Files.ReadWrite.All_: Write a file shared with the user (`PUT /users/rgregg@contoso.com/drive/root/children/file.txt/content`)</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1308">_Files.ReadWrite.AppFolder_：在 OneDrive 中将文件写入应用程序的文件夹 (`PUT /me/drive/special/approot/children/file.txt/content`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1308">_Files.ReadWrite.AppFolder_: Write files into the app's folder in OneDrive (`PUT /me/drive/special/approot/children/file.txt/content`)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1309">有关涉及多个权限的更复杂的情况，请参阅[权限方案](#permission-scenarios)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1309">For more complex scenarios involving multiple permissions, see [Permission scenarios](#permission-scenarios).</span></span>

### <a name="remarks"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1389">注解</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1389">Remarks</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1390">Microsoft 个人帐户不支持组功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1390">Group functionality is not supported on personal Microsoft accounts.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1391">Microsoft 365 组的组权限授予应用访问组内容的访问权限；例如，对话、文件、注释等。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1391">For Microsoft 365 groups, Group permissions grant the app access to the contents of the group; for example, conversations, files, notes, and so on.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-p161">应用程序权限对受支持的 API 有一些限制。有关详细信息，请参阅[已知问题](known-issues.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-p161">For application permissions, there are some limitations for the APIs that are supported. For more information, see [known issues](known-issues.md).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-p162">在某些情况下，应用可能需要 [目录权限](#directory-permissions)才能读取 `member` 和 `memberOf` 等组属性。例如，如果组将一个或多个 [servicePrincipals](/graph/api/resources/serviceprincipal?view=graph-rest-beta&preserve-view=true) 作为成员，则应用将需要有效权限才能通过授予的其中一个 _目录\*_ 权限读取服务主体，否则 Microsoft Graph 将返回错误。（如果是委派权限，已登录用户还需要组织的足够的权限才能读取服务主体。）相同的指导适用于 `memberOf` 属性，该属性可以返回 [administrativeUnits](/graph/api/resources/administrativeunit?view=graph-rest-beta&preserve-view=true)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-p162">In some cases, an app may need [Directory permissions](#directory-permissions) to read some group properties like `member` and `memberOf`. For example, if a group has a one or more [servicePrincipals](/graph/api/resources/serviceprincipal?view=graph-rest-beta&preserve-view=true) as members, the app will need effective permissions to read service principals through being granted one of the _Directory.\*_ permissions, otherwise Microsoft Graph will return an error. (In the case of delegated permissions, the signed-in user will also need sufficient privileges in the organization to read service principals.) The same guidance applies for the `memberOf` property, which can return [administrativeUnits](/graph/api/resources/administrativeunit?view=graph-rest-beta&preserve-view=true).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1397">要设置 Microsoft 365 组的 **preferredDataLocation** 属性，应用需要 Directory.ReadWrite.All 权限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1397">To set a Microsoft 365 group's **preferredDataLocation** attribute, an app needs Directory.ReadWrite.All permission.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1398">多地理位置环境中的用户创建 Microsoft 365 组时，该组的 **preferredDataLocation** 值将自动设置为该用户所使用的值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1398">When users in a multi-geo environment create a Microsoft 365 group, the **preferredDataLocation** value for the group is automatically set to that of the user.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1399">有关组的首选数据位置的详细信息，请参阅[使用特定 PDL 创建 Microsoft 365 组](/office365/enterprise/multi-geo-add-group-with-pdl)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1399">For more information about groups' preferred data location, see [Create a Microsoft 365 group with a specific PDL](/office365/enterprise/multi-geo-add-group-with-pdl).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-p164">组权限用于控制对 [Microsoft Teams](/graph/api/resources/teams-api-overview) 资源和 API 的访问权限。不支持 Microsoft 个人帐户。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-p164">Group permissions are used to control access to [Microsoft Teams](/graph/api/resources/teams-api-overview) resources and APIs. Personal Microsoft accounts are not supported.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-p165">组权限也用于控制对 [Microsoft Planner](/graph/api/resources/planner-overview) 资源和 API 的访问权限。Microsoft Planner API 仅支持委派权限，不支持应用程序权限。不支持 Microsoft 个人帐户。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-p165">Group permissions are also used to control access to [Microsoft Planner](/graph/api/resources/planner-overview) resources and APIs. Only delegated permissions are supported for Microsoft Planner APIs; application permissions are not supported. Personal Microsoft accounts are not supported.</span></span>


### <a name="example-usage"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1405">用法示例</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1405">Example usage</span></span>
#### <a name="delegated"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1406">Delegated</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1406">Delegated</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1407">_Group.Read.All_：读取登录用户所属的全部 Microsoft 365 组 (`GET /me/memberOf/$/microsoft.graph.group?$filter=groupTypes/any(a:a%20eq%20'unified')`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1407">_Group.Read.All_: Read all Microsoft 365 groups that the signed-in user is a member of (`GET /me/memberOf/$/microsoft.graph.group?$filter=groupTypes/any(a:a%20eq%20'unified')`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1408">_Group.Read.All_：读取诸如对话之类的所有 Microsoft 365 组内容 (`GET /groups/{id}/conversations`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1408">_Group.Read.All_: Read all Microsoft 365 group content like conversations (`GET /groups/{id}/conversations`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1409">_Group.ReadWrite.All_：更新组属性，如照片 (`PUT /groups/{id}/photo/$value`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1409">_Group.ReadWrite.All_: Update group properties, like photo (`PUT /groups/{id}/photo/$value`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1410">_GroupMember.ReadWrite.All_：更新组成员 (`POST /groups/{id}/members/$ref`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1410">_GroupMember.ReadWrite.All_: Update group members (`POST /groups/{id}/members/$ref`).</span></span>
> <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1411">**注意：** 这还要求 _User.ReadBasic.All_ 读取要作为成员添加的用户。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1411">**Note:**: This also requires _User.ReadBasic.All_ to read the user to add as a member.</span></span>

#### <a name="application"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1412">应用程序</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1412">Application</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1413">_Group.Read.All_：查找名称以“Sales”开头的所有组 (`GET /groups?$filter=startswith(displayName,'Sales')`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1413">_Group.Read.All_: Find all groups with name that starts with 'Sales' (`GET /groups?$filter=startswith(displayName,'Sales')`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1414">_Group.ReadWrite.All_：守护程序服务在 Microsoft 365 组日历上新建事件 (`POST /groups/{id}/events`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1414">_Group.ReadWrite.All_: Daemon service creates new events on a Microsoft 365 group's calendar (`POST /groups/{id}/events`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1415">_Group.Create_：创建新组 (`POST /groups`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1415">_Group.Create_: Creates a new group (`POST /groups`).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1416">有关涉及多个权限的更复杂的情况，请参阅[权限方案](#permission-scenarios)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1416">For more complex scenarios involving multiple permissions, see [Permission scenarios](#permission-scenarios).</span></span>
