### <a name="example-usage"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1438">用法示例</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1438">Example usage</span></span>

#### <a name="delegated"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1439">委派</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1439">Delegated</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1440">以下用法对两种委派权限均有效：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1440">The following usages are valid for both delegated permissions:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1441">_IdentityProvider.Read.All_：读取在租户中配置的所有标识提供程序 (`GET /beta/identityProviders`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1441">_IdentityProvider.Read.All_: Read all identity providers configured in the tenant (`GET /beta/identityProviders`)</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1442">_IdentityProvider.Read.All_：读取现有标识提供程序 (`GET /beta/identityProviders/{id}`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1442">_IdentityProvider.Read.All_: Read an existing identity provider (`GET /beta/identityProviders/{id}`)</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1443">_IdentityProvider.ReadWrite.All_：创建标识提供程序 (`POST /beta/identityProviders`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1443">_IdentityProvider.ReadWrite.All_ Create an identity provider (`POST /beta/identityProviders`)</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1444">_IdentityProvider.ReadWrite.All_：更新现有标识提供程序 (`PATCH /beta/identityProviders/{id}`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1444">_IdentityProvider.ReadWrite.All_ Update an existing identity provider (`PATCH /beta/identityProviders/{id}`)</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1445">_IdentityProvider.ReadWrite.All_：删除现有标识提供程序 (`DELETE /beta/identityProviders/{id}`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1445">_IdentityProvider.ReadWrite.All_ Delete an existing identity provider (`DELETE /beta/identityProviders/{id}`)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1446">有关涉及多个权限的更复杂的情况，请参阅[权限方案](#permission-scenarios)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1446">For more complex scenarios involving multiple permissions, see [Permission scenarios](#permission-scenarios).</span></span>

### <a name="remarks"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1468">注解</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1468">Remarks</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-p167">_IdentityRiskEvent.Read.All_ 仅适用于工作或学校帐户。对于通过委派权限读取标识风险信息的应用，登录用户必须是以下管理员角色之一的成员：全局管理员、安全管理员或安全读者。有关管理员角色的详细信息，请参阅 [在 Azure Active Directory 中分配管理员角色](/azure/active-directory/active-directory-assign-admin-roles)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-p167">_IdentityRiskEvent.Read.All_ is valid only for work or school accounts. For an app with delegated permissions to read identity risk information, the signed-in user must be a member of one of the following administrator roles: Global Administrator, Security Administrator, or Security Reader. For more information about administrator roles, see [Assigning administrator roles in Azure Active Directory](/azure/active-directory/active-directory-assign-admin-roles).</span></span>

### <a name="example-usage"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1472">用法示例</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1472">Example usage</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1474">以下用法对委派权限和应用程序权限均有效：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1474">The following usages are valid for both delegated and application permissions:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1475">读取为租户中的所有用户所生成的全部风险事件 (`GET /beta/identityRiskEvents`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1475">Read all risk events generated for all users in the tenant (`GET /beta/identityRiskEvents`)</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1476">读取由 Dorknet 僵尸网络所生成的恶意软件风险事件 (`GET /beta/malwareRiskEvents?$filter=malwareName eq 'Dorkbot'`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1476">Read malware risk events generated by the Dorknet botnet (`GET /beta/malwareRiskEvents?$filter=malwareName eq 'Dorkbot'`)</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1505">_IdentityRiskyUser.ReadWrite.All_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1505">_IdentityRiskyUser.ReadWrite.All_</span></span> |   <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1506">读取和更新标识用户风险信息</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1506">Read and update identity user risk  information</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1507">允许应用在没有登录用户的情况下读取和更新组织中所有用户的标识用户风险信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1507">Allows the app to read and update identity user risk information for all users in your organization without a signed-in user.</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1508">是</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1508">Yes</span></span> |


### <a name="remarks"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1509">说明</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1509">Remarks</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1510">_IdentityRiskyUser.Read.All_ 和 _IdentityRiskyUser.ReadWrite.ALL_ 仅适用于工作或学校帐户。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1510">_IdentityRiskyUser.Read.All_ and _IdentityRiskyUser.ReadWrite.ALL_ is valid only for work or school accounts.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1511">对于通过委派权限读取标识用户风险信息的应用，登录用户必须是以下管理员角色之一的成员：全局管理员、安全管理员或安全读者。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1511">For an app with delegated permissions to read identity user risk information, the signed-in user must be a member of one of the following administrator roles: Global Administrator, Security Administrator, or Security Reader.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1512">若要详细了解管理员角色，请参阅[在 Azure Active Directory 中分配管理员角色](/azure/active-directory/active-directory-assign-admin-roles)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1512">For more information about administrator roles, see [Assigning administrator roles in Azure Active Directory](/azure/active-directory/active-directory-assign-admin-roles).</span></span>

### <a name="example-usage"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1513">用法示例</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1513">Example usage</span></span>

#### <a name="delegated-and-application"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1514">委派和应用程序</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1514">Delegated and Application</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1515">以下用法对委派权限和应用程序权限均有效：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1515">The following usages are valid for both delegated and application permissions:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1516">读取租户中的所有风险用户和属性 (`GET /beta/riskyUsers`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1516">Read all risky users and properties in the tenant (`GET /beta/riskyUsers`)</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1517">读取所有聚合风险级别为中等的风险用户 (`GET /beta/riskyUsers?$filter=risk/riskLevelAggregated eq microsoft.graph.riskLevel'medium'`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1517">Read all risky users whose aggregate risk level is Medium (`GET /beta/riskyUsers?$filter=risk/riskLevelAggregated eq microsoft.graph.riskLevel'medium'`)</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1518">阅读特定用户的风险信息 (`GET /beta/riskyUsers/$filter=id eq ‘{userObjectId}’`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1518">Read the risk information for a specific user (`GET /beta/riskyUsers/$filter=id eq ‘{userObjectId}’`)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1519">有关涉及多个权限的更复杂的情况，请参阅[权限方案](#permission-scenarios)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1519">For more complex scenarios involving multiple permissions, see [Permission scenarios](#permission-scenarios).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1557">若要详细了解管理员角色，请参阅[在 Azure Active Directory 中分配管理员角色](/azure/active-directory/active-directory-assign-admin-roles)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1557">For more information about administrator roles, see [Assigning administrator roles in Azure Active Directory](/azure/active-directory/active-directory-assign-admin-roles).</span></span>

### <a name="example-usage"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1558">用法示例</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1558">Example usage</span></span>

#### <a name="delegated-and-application"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1559">委派和应用程序</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1559">Delegated and Application</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1560">以下用法对委派权限和应用程序权限均有效：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1560">The following usages are valid for both delegated and application permissions:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1561">_IdentityUserFlow.Read.All_：读取 Azure AD B2C 租户中的所有用户流 (`GET beta/identity/b2cUserFlows`) </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1561">_IdentityUserFlow.Read.All_: Read all user flows in an Azure AD B2C tenant (`GET beta/identity/b2cUserFlows`)</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1562">_IdentityUserFlow.Read.All_：读取 Azure Active Directory (Azure AD) 租户中的所有用户流 (`GET beta/identity/b2xUserFlows`) </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1562">_IdentityUserFlow.Read.All_: Read all user flows in an Azure Active Directory (Azure AD) tenant (`GET beta/identity/b2xUserFlows`)</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1563">_IdentityUserFlow.Read.All_：读取 Azure AD B2C 用户流中的所有用户属性分配（`GET beta/identity/b2cUserFlows/{id}/userAttributeAssignments`） </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1563">_IdentityUserFlow.Read.All_: Read all user attribute assignments in an Azure AD B2C user flow (`GET beta/identity/b2cUserFlows/{id}/userAttributeAssignments`)</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1564">_IdentityUserFlow.ReadWrite.All_：在 Azure AD B2C 租户中创建新用户流 (`POST beta/identity/b2cUserFlows`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1564">_IdentityUserFlow.ReadWrite.All_: Create a new user flow in an Azure AD B2C tenant (`POST beta/identity/b2cUserFlows`)</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1565">_IdentityUserFlow.ReadWrite.All_：在 Azure Active Directory (Azure AD) 租户中创建新用户流 (`POST beta/identity/b2xUserflows`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1565">_IdentityUserFlow.ReadWrite.All_: Create a new user flow in an Azure Active Directory (Azure AD) tenant (`POST beta/identity/b2xUserflows`)</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1566">_IdentitytUserFlow.ReadWrite.All_：将标识提供者添加到 Azure AD B2C 用户流 (`PATCH beta/identity/b2cUserFlows/{id}/identityProviders/$ref`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1566">_IdentitytUserFlow.ReadWrite.All_: Add an identity provider to an Azure AD B2C user flow (`PATCH beta/identity/b2cUserFlows/{id}/identityProviders/$ref`)</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1567">_IdentityUserFlow.ReadWrite.All_：从 Azure AD B2C 用户流中删除标识提供者 (`DELETE beta/identity/b2cUserFlows/{id}/identityProviders/{id}`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1567">_IdentityUserFlow.ReadWrite.All_: Remove an identity provider from an Azure AD B2C user flow (`DELETE beta/identity/b2cUserFlows/{id}/identityProviders/{id}`)</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1568">_IdentityUserFlow.ReadWrite.All_：在 Azure AD B2C 用户流中创建用户属性分配（`POST beta/identity/b2cUserFlows/{id}/userAttributeAssignments`）</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1568">_IdentityUserFlow.ReadWrite.All_: Create a user attribute assignment in an Azure AD B2C user flow (`POST beta/identity/b2cUserFlows/{id}/userAttributeAssignments`)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1569">有关涉及多个权限的更复杂的情况，请参阅[权限方案](#permission-scenarios)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1569">For more complex scenarios involving multiple permissions, see [Permission scenarios](#permission-scenarios).</span></span>

|<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1706">_DeviceManagementServiceConfig.Read.All_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1706">_DeviceManagementServiceConfig.Read.All_</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1707">读取 Microsoft Intune 配置</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1707">Read Microsoft Intune configuration</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1708">允许应用读取 Intune 服务属性，其中包括设备注册和第三方服务连接配置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1708">Allows the app to read Intune service properties including device enrollment and third party service connection configuration.</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1709">是</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1709">Yes</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1710">否</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1710">No</span></span> |
|<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1711">_DeviceManagementServiceConfig.ReadWrite.All_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1711">_DeviceManagementServiceConfig.ReadWrite.All_</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1712">读取和写入 Microsoft Intune 配置</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1712">Read and write Microsoft Intune configuration</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1713">允许应用读取和写入 Microsoft Intune 服务属性，其中包括设备注册和第三方服务连接配置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1713">Allows the app to read and write Microsoft Intune service properties including device enrollment and third party service connection configuration.</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1714">是</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1714">Yes</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1715">否</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1715">No</span></span> |

### <a name="remarks"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1716">注解</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1716">Remarks</span></span>

> <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1717">**注意：** 使用 Microsoft Graph API 配置 Intune 控件和策略仍需要客户 [正确许可](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=839381) Intune 服务。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1717">**Note:** Using the Microsoft Graph APIs to configure Intune controls and policies still requires that the Intune service is [correctly licensed](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=839381) by the customer.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1718">这些权限仅对工作或学校帐户有效。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1718">These permissions are only valid for work or school accounts.</span></span>

### <a name="example-usage"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1719">用法示例</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1719">Example usage</span></span>

#### <a name="delegated"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1720">委派</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1720">Delegated</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1721">_DeviceManagementServiceConfiguration.Read.All_：检查 Intune 订阅的当前状态 (`GET /deviceManagement/subscriptionState`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1721">_DeviceManagementServiceConfiguration.Read.All_: Check the current state of the Intune subscription (`GET /deviceManagement/subscriptionState`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1722">_DeviceManagementServiceConfiguration.ReadWrite.All_：新建条款和条件 (`POST /deviceManagement/termsAndConditions`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1722">_DeviceManagementServiceConfiguration.ReadWrite.All_: Create new Terms and Conditions (`POST /deviceManagement/termsAndConditions`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1723">_DeviceManagementConfiguration.Read.All_：查找设备配置状态 (`GET /deviceManagement/deviceConfigurations/{id}/deviceStatuses`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1723">_DeviceManagementConfiguration.Read.All_: Find the status of a device configuration (`GET /deviceManagement/deviceConfigurations/{id}/deviceStatuses`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1724">_DeviceManagementConfiguration.ReadWrite.All_：向组分配设备符合性策略 (`POST deviceCompliancePolicies/{id}/assign`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1724">_DeviceManagementConfiguration.ReadWrite.All_: Assign a device compliance policy to a group (`POST deviceCompliancePolicies/{id}/assign`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1725">_DeviceManagementApps.Read.All_：查找发布到 Intune 的所有 Windows 应用商店应用 (`GET /deviceAppManagement/mobileApps?$filter=isOf('microsoft.graph.windowsStoreApp')`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1725">_DeviceManagementApps.Read.All_: Find all the Windows Store apps published to Intune (`GET /deviceAppManagement/mobileApps?$filter=isOf('microsoft.graph.windowsStoreApp')`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1726">_DeviceManagementApps.ReadWrite.All_：发布新应用程序 (`POST /deviceAppManagement/mobileApps`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1726">_DeviceManagementApps.ReadWrite.All_: Publish a new application (`POST /deviceAppManagement/mobileApps`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1727">_DeviceManagementRBAC.Read.All_：按名称查找角色分配 (`GET /deviceManagement/roleAssignments?$filter=displayName eq 'My Role Assignment'`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1727">_DeviceManagementRBAC.Read.All_: Find a role assignment by name (`GET /deviceManagement/roleAssignments?$filter=displayName eq 'My Role Assignment'`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1728">_DeviceManagementRBAC.ReadWrite.All_：新建自定义角色 (`POST /deviceManagement/roleDefinitions`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1728">_DeviceManagementRBAC.ReadWrite.All_: Create a new custom role (`POST /deviceManagement/roleDefinitions`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1729">_DeviceManagementManagedDevices.Read.All_：按名称查找受管理设备 (`GET /managedDevices/?$filter=deviceName eq 'My Device'`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1729">_DeviceManagementManagedDevices.Read.All_: Find a managed device by name (`GET /managedDevices/?$filter=deviceName eq 'My Device'`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1730">_DeviceManagementManagedDevices.ReadWrite.All_：删除受管理设备 (`DELETE /managedDevices/{id}`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1730">_DeviceManagementManagedDevices.ReadWrite.All_: Remove a managed device (`DELETE /managedDevices/{id}`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1731">_DeviceManagementManagedDevices.PrivilegedOperations.All_：重置用户的受管理设备上的密码 (`POST /managedDevices/{id}/resetPasscode`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1731">_DeviceManagementManagedDevices.PrivilegedOperations.All_: Reset the passcode on a user's managed device (`POST /managedDevices/{id}/resetPasscode`).</span></span>

#### <a name="application"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1732">应用程序</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1732">Application</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1733">_DeviceManagementServiceConfiguration.Read.All_：检查 Intune 订阅的当前状态 (`GET /deviceManagement/subscriptionState`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1733">_DeviceManagementServiceConfiguration.Read.All_: Check the current state of the Intune subscription (`GET /deviceManagement/subscriptionState`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1734">_DeviceManagementServiceConfiguration.ReadWrite.All_：新建条款和条件 (`POST /deviceManagement/termsAndConditions`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1734">_DeviceManagementServiceConfiguration.ReadWrite.All_: Create new Terms and Conditions (`POST /deviceManagement/termsAndConditions`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1735">_DeviceManagementConfiguration.Read.All_：查找设备配置状态 (`GET /deviceManagement/deviceConfigurations/{id}/deviceStatuses`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1735">_DeviceManagementConfiguration.Read.All_: Find the status of a device configuration (`GET /deviceManagement/deviceConfigurations/{id}/deviceStatuses`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1736">_DeviceManagementConfiguration.ReadWrite.All_：向组分配设备符合性策略 (`POST deviceCompliancePolicies/{id}/assign`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1736">_DeviceManagementConfiguration.ReadWrite.All_: Assign a device compliance policy to a group (`POST deviceCompliancePolicies/{id}/assign`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1737">_DeviceManagementApps.Read.All_：查找发布到 Intune 的所有 Windows 应用商店应用 (`GET /deviceAppManagement/mobileApps?$filter=isOf('microsoft.graph.windowsStoreApp')`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1737">_DeviceManagementApps.Read.All_: Find all the Windows Store apps published to Intune (`GET /deviceAppManagement/mobileApps?$filter=isOf('microsoft.graph.windowsStoreApp')`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1738">_DeviceManagementApps.ReadWrite.All_：发布新应用程序 (`POST /deviceAppManagement/mobileApps`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1738">_DeviceManagementApps.ReadWrite.All_: Publish a new application (`POST /deviceAppManagement/mobileApps`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1739">_DeviceManagementRBAC.Read.All_：按名称查找角色分配 (`GET /deviceManagement/roleAssignments?$filter=displayName eq 'My Role Assignment'`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1739">_DeviceManagementRBAC.Read.All_: Find a role assignment by name (`GET /deviceManagement/roleAssignments?$filter=displayName eq 'My Role Assignment'`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1740">_DeviceManagementRBAC.ReadWrite.All_：新建自定义角色 (`POST /deviceManagement/roleDefinitions`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1740">_DeviceManagementRBAC.ReadWrite.All_: Create a new custom role (`POST /deviceManagement/roleDefinitions`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1741">_DeviceManagementManagedDevices.Read.All_：按名称查找受管理设备 (`GET /managedDevices/?$filter=deviceName eq 'My Device'`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1741">_DeviceManagementManagedDevices.Read.All_: Find a managed device by name (`GET /managedDevices/?$filter=deviceName eq 'My Device'`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1742">_DeviceManagementManagedDevices.ReadWrite.All_：删除受管理设备 (`DELETE /managedDevices/{id}`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1742">_DeviceManagementManagedDevices.ReadWrite.All_: Remove a managed device (`DELETE /managedDevices/{id}`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1743">_DeviceManagementManagedDevices.PrivilegedOperations.All_：重置用户的受管理设备上的密码 (`POST /managedDevices/{id}/resetPasscode`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1743">_DeviceManagementManagedDevices.PrivilegedOperations.All_: Reset the passcode on a user's managed device (`POST /managedDevices/{id}/resetPasscode`).</span></span>

### <a name="remarks"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1853">说明</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1853">Remarks</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-p183">_Mail.Read.Shared_、_Mail.ReadWrite.Shared_ 和 _Mail.Send.Shared_ 仅适用于工作或学校帐户。所有其他权限对于 Microsoft 帐户和工作或学校帐户均有效。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-p183">_Mail.Read.Shared_, _Mail.ReadWrite.Shared_, and _Mail.Send.Shared_ are only valid for work or school accounts. All other permissions are valid for both Microsoft accounts and work or school accounts.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1856">通过 _Mail.Send_ 或 _Mail.Send.Shared_ 权限，应用可以发送邮件并将副本保存到用户的“已发送邮件”文件夹中，即使应用不使用相应的 _Mail.ReadWrite_ 或 _Mail.ReadWrite.Shared_ 权限也是如此。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1856">With the _Mail.Send_ or _Mail.Send.Shared_ permission, an app can send mail and save a copy to the user's Sent Items folder, even if the app does not use a corresponding _Mail.ReadWrite_ or _Mail.ReadWrite.Shared_ permission.</span></span>

### <a name="example-usage"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1857">用法示例</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1857">Example usage</span></span>

#### <a name="delegated"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1858">委派</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1858">Delegated</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1859">_Mail.Read_：列出用户收件箱中的邮件，按 `receivedDateTime` 排序 (`GET /me/mailfolders/inbox/messages?$orderby=receivedDateTime DESC`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1859">_Mail.Read_: List messages in the user's inbox, sorted by `receivedDateTime` (`GET /me/mailfolders/inbox/messages?$orderby=receivedDateTime DESC`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1860">_Mail.Read.Shared_：在已与登录用户共享其收件箱的用户收件箱中查找带有附件的所有邮件 (`GET /users{id | userPrincipalName}/mailfolders/inbox/messages?$filter=hasAttachments eq true`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1860">_Mail.Read.Shared_: Find all messages with attachments in a user's inbox that has shared their inbox with the signed-in user (`GET /users{id | userPrincipalName}/mailfolders/inbox/messages?$filter=hasAttachments eq true`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1861">_Mail.ReadWrite_：将邮件标记为已读 (`PATCH /me/messages/{id}`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1861">_Mail.ReadWrite_: Mark a message read (`PATCH /me/messages/{id}`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1862">_Mail.Send_：发送邮件 (`POST /me/sendmail`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1862">_Mail.Send_: Send a message (`POST /me/sendmail`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1863">_MailboxSettings.ReadWrite_：更新用户的自动答复 (`PATCH /me/mailboxSettings`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1863">_MailboxSettings.ReadWrite_: Update the user's automatic reply (`PATCH /me/mailboxSettings`).</span></span>

#### <a name="application"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1864">应用程序</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1864">Application</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1865">_Mail.Read_：从 bob@contoso.com 查找邮件 (`GET /users/{id | userPrincipalName}/messages?$filter=from/emailAddress/address eq 'bob@contoso.com'`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1865">_Mail.Read_: Find messages from bob@contoso.com (`GET /users/{id | userPrincipalName}/messages?$filter=from/emailAddress/address eq 'bob@contoso.com'`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1866">_Mail.ReadWrite_：在名为“`Expense Reports`”的收件箱中新建文件夹 (`POST /users/{id | userPrincipalName}/mailfolders`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1866">_Mail.ReadWrite_: Create a new folder in the Inbox named `Expense Reports` (`POST /users/{id | userPrincipalName}/mailfolders`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1867">_Mail.Send_：发送邮件 (`POST /users/{id | userPrincipalName}/sendmail`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1867">_Mail.Send_: Send a message (`POST /users/{id | userPrincipalName}/sendmail`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1868">_MailboxSettings.Read_：获取用户邮箱的默认时区 (`GET /users/{id | userPrincipalName}/mailboxSettings/timeZone`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1868">_MailboxSettings.Read_: Get the default timezone for the user's mailbox (`GET /users/{id | userPrincipalName}/mailboxSettings/timeZone`)</span></span>


<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1869">有关涉及多个权限的更复杂的情况，请参阅[权限方案](#permission-scenarios)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1869">For more complex scenarios involving multiple permissions, see [Permission scenarios](#permission-scenarios).</span></span>

### <a name="remarks"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1891">注释</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1891">Remarks</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1892">_Member.Read.Hidden_ 仅对工作或学校帐户有效。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1892">_Member.Read.Hidden_ is valid only on work or school accounts.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-p184">可以隐藏某些 Microsoft 365 组中的成员资格。这意味着只有该组的成员可以查看其成员。此功能可用于帮助遵守要求组织对外部用户（例如，表示某个班级内注册的学生的 Microsoft 365 组）隐藏组成员身份的规定。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-p184">Membership in some Microsoft 365 groups can be hidden. This means that only the members of the group can view its members. This feature can be used to help comply with regulations that require an organization to hide group membership from outsiders (for example, a Microsoft 365 group that represents students enrolled in a class).</span></span>

### <a name="example-usage"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1896">用法示例</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1896">Example usage</span></span>

#### <a name="delegated"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1897">委派</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1897">Delegated</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1898">_Member.Read.Hidden_：代表登录用户读取隐藏了成员资格的管理单元成员 (`GET /administrativeUnits/{id}/members`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1898">_Member.Read.Hidden_: Read the members of an administrative unit with hidden membership on behalf of the signed-in user (`GET /administrativeUnits/{id}/members`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1899">_Member.Read.Hidden_：代表登录用户读取隐藏了成员资格的组成员 (`GET /groups/{id}/members`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1899">_Member.Read.Hidden_: Read the members of a group with hidden membership on behalf of the signed-in user (`GET /groups/{id}/members`).</span></span>

#### <a name="application"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1900">应用程序</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1900">Application</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1901">_Member.Read.Hidden_：读取隐藏了成员资格的管理单元成员 (`GET /administrativeUnits/{id}/members`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1901">_Member.Read.Hidden_: Read the members of an administrative unit with hidden membership (`GET /administrativeUnits/{id}/members`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1902">_Member.Read.Hidden_：读取隐藏了成员资格的组成员 (`GET /groups/{id}/members`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1902">_Member.Read.Hidden_: Read the members of a group with hidden membership (`GET /groups/{id}/members`).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1903">有关涉及多个权限的更复杂的情况，请参阅[权限方案](#permission-scenarios)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1903">For more complex scenarios involving multiple permissions, see [Permission scenarios](#permission-scenarios).</span></span>

### <a name="remarks"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1956">注解</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1956">Remarks</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-p186">_Notes.Read.All_ 和 _Notes.ReadWrite.All_ 仅适用于工作或学校帐户。所有其他权限对于 Microsoft 帐户和工作或学校帐户均有效。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-p186">_Notes.Read.All_ and _Notes.ReadWrite.All_ are only valid for work or school accounts. All other permissions are valid for both Microsoft accounts and work or school accounts.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1959">通过 _Notes.Create_ 权限，应用可以查看已登录用户的 OneNote 笔记本层次结构，并创建 OneNote 内容（笔记本、分区组、分区、页面等）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1959">With the _Notes.Create_ permission, an app can view the OneNote notebook hierarchy of the signed-in user and create OneNote content (notebooks, section groups, sections, pages, etc.).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1960">_Notes.ReadWrite_ 和 _Notes.ReadWrite.All_ 还允许应用修改针对已登录用户可以访问的 OneNote 内容的权限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1960">_Notes.ReadWrite_ and _Notes.ReadWrite.All_ also allow the app to modify the permissions on the OneNote content that can be accessed by the signed-in user.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1961">对于工作或学校帐户，_Notes.Read.All_ 和 _Notes.ReadWrite.All_ 允许该应用访问已登录用户有权限在组织内访问的其他用户的 OneNote 内容。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1961">For work or school accounts, _Notes.Read.All_ and _Notes.ReadWrite.All_ allow the app to access other users' OneNote content that the signed-in user has permission to within the organization.</span></span>

### <a name="example-usage"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1962">用法示例</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1962">Example usage</span></span>
#### <a name="delegated"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1963">委派</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1963">Delegated</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1964">_Notes.Create_：为登录用户新建笔记本 (`POST /me/onenote/notebooks`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1964">_Notes.Create_: Create a new notebooks for the signed-in user (`POST /me/onenote/notebooks`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1965">_Notes.Read_：读取登录用户的笔记本 (`GET /me/onenote/notebooks`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1965">_Notes.Read_: Read the notebooks for the signed-in user (`GET /me/onenote/notebooks`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1966">_Notes.Read.All_：获取登录用户有权在组织内访问的所有笔记本 (`GET /me/onenote/notebooks?includesharednotebooks=true`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1966">_Notes.Read.All_: Get all notebooks that the signed-in user has access to within the organization (`GET /me/onenote/notebooks?includesharednotebooks=true`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1967">_Notes.ReadWrite_：更新登录用户的页面 (`PATCH /me/onenote/pages/{id}/$value`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1967">_Notes.ReadWrite_: Update the page of the signed-in user (`PATCH /me/onenote/pages/{id}/$value`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1968">_Notes.ReadWrite.All_：在登录用户有权在组织内访问的其他用户笔记本中创建页面 (`POST /users/{id}/onenote/pages`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1968">_Notes.ReadWrite.All_: Create a page in another user's notebook that the signed-in user has access to within the organization (`POST /users/{id}/onenote/pages`).</span></span>

#### <a name="application"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1969">应用程序</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1969">Application</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1970">_Notes.Read.All_：读取组中的所有用户笔记本 (`GET /groups/{id}/onenote/notebooks`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1970">_Notes.Read.All_: Read all users notebooks in a group (`GET /groups/{id}/onenote/notebooks`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1971">_Notes.ReadWrite.All_：更新组织中任意用户的笔记本中的页面 (`PATCH /users/{id}/onenote/pages/{id}/$value`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1971">_Notes.ReadWrite.All_: Update the page in a notebook for any user in the organization (`PATCH /users/{id}/onenote/pages/{id}/$value`).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1972">有关涉及多个权限的更复杂的情况，请参阅[权限方案](#permission-scenarios)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1972">For more complex scenarios involving multiple permissions, see [Permission scenarios](#permission-scenarios).</span></span>

#### <a name="delegated-permissions"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1974">委派权限</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1974">Delegated permissions</span></span>

|:-----------------------------|:-----------------------------------------|:-----------------|:-----------------|
| <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1979">_Notifications.ReadWrite.CreatedByApp_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1979">_Notifications.ReadWrite.CreatedByApp_</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1980">提供和管理此应用的通知。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1980">Deliver and manage notifications for this app.</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1981">允许应用代表登录用户提供其通知。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1981">Allow the app to deliver its notifications on behalf of signed-in users.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1982">此外，还允许应用读取、更新和删除此应用的用户通知项目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1982">Also allows the app to read, update, and delete the user’s notification items for this app.</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1983">否</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1983">No</span></span> |
### <a name="remarks"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1984">注解</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1984">Remarks</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1985">*Notifications.ReadWrite.CreatedByApp* 对 Microsoft 帐户和工作或学校帐户均有效。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1985">*Notifications.ReadWrite.CreatedByApp* is valid for both Microsoft accounts and work or school accounts.</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1986">与此权限相关联的 *CreatedByApp* 约束指示服务将基于通话应用的标识（Microsoft 帐户应用 ID 或针对跨平台应用程序标识配置的一组应用 ID）对结果应用隐式筛选。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1986">The *CreatedByApp* constraint associated with this permission indicates that the service will apply implicit filtering to results based on the identity of the calling app, either the Microsoft account app ID or a set of app IDs configured for a cross-platform application identity.</span></span>
### <a name="example-usage"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1987">用法示例</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1987">Example usage</span></span>
#### <a name="delegated"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1988">委派</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1988">Delegated</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1989">_Notifications.ReadWrite.CreatedByApp_：发布以用户为中心的通知，然后可能会将该通知传递至用户运行在不同端点上的多个应用程序客户端。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1989">_Notifications.ReadWrite.CreatedByApp_: Publish a user-centric notification, which might then be delivered to the user’s multiple application clients running on different endpoints.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1990">(POST /me/notifications/)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1990">(POST /me/notifications/).</span></span>

## <a name="online-meetings-permissions"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1991">联机会议权限</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1991">Online meetings permissions</span></span>

#### <a name="delegated-permissions"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ca75-1992">委派权限</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-1992">Delegated permissions</span></span>

### <a name="example-usage"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ca75-2022">用法示例</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-2022">Example usage</span></span>

#### <a name="delegated"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ca75-2023">委派</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-2023">Delegated</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-2024">_OnlineMeetings.Read_：检索 [联机会议](/graph/api/onlinemeeting-get?view=graph-rest-beta&preserve-view=true)的属性和关系 (`GET /beta/communications/onlinemeetings/{default id}`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-2024">_OnlineMeetings.Read_: Retrieve the properties and relationships of an [online meeting](/graph/api/onlinemeeting-get?view=graph-rest-beta&preserve-view=true) (`GET /beta/communications/onlinemeetings/{default id}`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-2025">_OnlineMeetings.ReadWrite_：创建 [联机会议](/graph/api/application-post-onlinemeetings?view=graph-rest-beta&preserve-view=true) (`POST /beta/communications/onlinemeetings`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-2025">_OnlineMeetings.ReadWrite_: Create an [online meeting](/graph/api/application-post-onlinemeetings?view=graph-rest-beta&preserve-view=true) (`POST /beta/communications/onlinemeetings`).</span></span>

#### <a name="application"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ca75-2026">应用程序</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-2026">Application</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-2027">_OnlineMeetings.Read.All_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-2027">_OnlineMeetings.Read.All_</span></span>
  * <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-2028">检索[联机会议](/graph/api/onlinemeeting-get?view=graph-rest-beta&preserve-view=true)的属性和关系 (`GET /beta/communications/onlinemeetings/?$filter=VideoTeleconferenceId%20eq%20'{id}'`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-2028">Retrieve the properties and relationships of an [online meeting](/graph/api/onlinemeeting-get?view=graph-rest-beta&preserve-view=true) (`GET /beta/communications/onlinemeetings/?$filter=VideoTeleconferenceId%20eq%20'{id}'`).</span></span>
  * <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-2029">代表用户检索[联机会议](/graph/api/onlinemeeting-get?view=graph-rest-beta&preserve-view=true) (\`GET /beta/users/{userId}/onlineMeetings/{id})</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-2029">Retrieve an [online meeting](/graph/api/onlinemeeting-get?view=graph-rest-beta&preserve-view=true) on behalf of a user (\`GET /beta/users/{userId}/onlineMeetings/{id})</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-2030">_OnlineMeetings.ReadWrite.All_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-2030">_OnlineMeetings.ReadWrite.All_</span></span>
  * <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-2031">代表用户创建[联机会议](/graph/api/onlinemeeting-get?view=graph-rest-beta&preserve-view=true) (\`POST /beta/users/{userId}/onlineMeetings/)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-2031">Create an [online meeting](/graph/api/onlinemeeting-get?view=graph-rest-beta&preserve-view=true) on behalf of a user (\`POST /beta/users/{userId}/onlineMeetings/)</span></span>
  * <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-2032">代表用户更新[联机会议](/graph/api/onlinemeeting-get?view=graph-rest-beta&preserve-view=true) (\`PATCH /beta/users/{userId}/onlineMeetings/{id})</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-2032">Update an [online meeting](/graph/api/onlinemeeting-get?view=graph-rest-beta&preserve-view=true) on behalf of a user (\`PATCH /beta/users/{userId}/onlineMeetings/{id})</span></span>
  * <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-2033">代表用户删除[联机会议](/graph/api/onlinemeeting-get?view=graph-rest-beta&preserve-view=true) (\`DELETE /beta/users/{userId}/onlineMeetings/{id})</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-2033">Delete an [online meeting](/graph/api/onlinemeeting-get?view=graph-rest-beta&preserve-view=true) on behalf of a user (\`DELETE /beta/users/{userId}/onlineMeetings/{id})</span></span>
  
> <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-2034">**注意**：创建 [联机会议](/graph/api/application-post-onlinemeetings?view=graph-rest-beta&preserve-view=true)时会代表用户创建一个会议，但不会在该用户的日历上显示该会议。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-2034">**Note**: Creating an [online meeting](/graph/api/application-post-onlinemeetings?view=graph-rest-beta&preserve-view=true) creates a meeting on behalf of a user, but does not show it on the user's Calendar.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-2035">有关涉及多个权限的更复杂的情况，请参阅[权限方案](#permission-scenarios)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-2035">For more complex scenarios involving multiple permissions, see [Permission scenarios](#permission-scenarios).</span></span>

### <a name="remarks"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ca75-2088">注解</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-2088">Remarks</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-p190">可以使用这些权限指定要在 Azure AD 授权和令牌请求中返回的项目。Azure AD v1.0 和 v2.0 终结点以不同的方式支持它们。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-p190">You can use these permissions to specify artifacts that you want returned in Azure AD authorization and token requests. They are supported differently by the Azure AD v1.0 and v2.0 endpoints.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-p191">使用 Azure AD (v1.0) 终结点时，仅使用 _openid_ 权限。在授权请求的 *scope* 参数中指定它，以在使用 OpenID Connect 协议让用户登录应用时返回 ID 令牌。有关详细信息，请参阅 [使用 OpenID Connect 和 Azure Active Directory 来授权访问 Web 应用程序](/azure/active-directory/develop/active-directory-protocols-openid-connect-code)。若要成功返回 ID 令牌，还必须确保在注册应用时已配置 _User.Read_ 权限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-p191">With the Azure AD (v1.0) endpoint, only the _openid_ permission is used. You specify it in the *scope* parameter in an authorization request to return an ID token when you use the OpenID Connect protocol to sign in a user to your app. For more information, see [Authorize access to web applications using OpenID Connect and Azure Active Directory](/azure/active-directory/develop/active-directory-protocols-openid-connect-code). To successfully return an ID token, you must also make sure that the _User.Read_ permission is configured when you register your app.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-p192">使用 Azure AD v2.0 终结点时，在 _scope_ 参数中指定 _offline\_access_ 权限，以在使用 OAuth 2.0 或 OpenID Connect 协议时显式请求获取刷新令牌。使用 OpenID Connect 时，指定 _openid_ 权限来请求获取 ID 令牌。还可指定 _email_ 权限和/或 _profile_ 权限，以在 ID 令牌中返回其他声明。使用 v2.0 终结点时，无需指定 _User.Read_ 来返回 ID 令牌。有关详细信息，请参阅 [OpenID Connect 作用域](/azure/active-directory/develop/active-directory-v2-scopes#openid-connect-scopes)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-p192">With the Azure AD v2.0 endpoint, you specify the _offline\_access_ permission in the _scope_ parameter to explicitly request a refresh token when using the OAuth 2.0 or OpenID Connect protocols. With OpenID Connect, you specify the _openid_ permission to request an ID token. You can also specify the _email_ permission, _profile_ permission, or both to return additional claims in the ID token. You do not need to specify _User.Read_ to return an ID token with the v2.0 endpoint. For more information, see [OpenID Connect scopes](/azure/active-directory/develop/active-directory-v2-scopes#openid-connect-scopes).</span></span>

> <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-p193">**重要说明**：目前，Microsoft 身份验证库 (MSAL) 默认在授权和令牌请求中指定 _offline\_access_、_openid_、_profile_ 和 _email_。也就是说，在默认情况下，如果显式指定这些权限，Azure AD 可能会返回错误。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-p193">**Important** The Microsoft Authentication Library (MSAL) currently specifies _offline\_access_, _openid_, _profile_, and _email_ by default in authorization and token requests. This means that, for the default case, if you specify these permissions explicitly, Azure AD may return an error.</span></span>

### <a name="remarks"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ca75-2199">备注</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-2199">Remarks</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-2200">People.Read.All 权限仅适用于工作和学校帐户。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-2200">The People.Read.All permission is only valid for work and school accounts.</span></span>

### <a name="example-usage"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ca75-2201">用法示例</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-2201">Example usage</span></span>

#### <a name="delegated"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ca75-2202">委派</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-2202">Delegated</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-2203">_People.Read_：读取相关人员列表 (`GET /me/people`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-2203">_People.Read_: Read a list of relevant people (`GET /me/people`)</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-2204">_People.Read.All_：读取同一组织中与其他用户相关的人员列表 (`GET /users('{id})/people`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-2204">_People.Read.All_: Read a list of relevant people to another user in the same organization (`GET /users('{id})/people`)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-2205">有关涉及多个权限的更复杂的情况，请参阅[权限方案](#permission-scenarios)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-2205">For more complex scenarios involving multiple permissions, see [Permission scenarios](#permission-scenarios).</span></span>

### <a name="example-usage"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ca75-2406">用法示例</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-2406">Example usage</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-2407">以下用法对委派权限和应用程序权限均有效：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-2407">The following usages are valid for both delegated and application permissions:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-2408">_Policy.Read.All_ 读取你所在组织的策略 (`GET /policies`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-2408">_Policy.Read.All_: Read your organization's policies (`GET /policies`)</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-2409">_Policy.Read.All_ 读取你所在组织的信任框架策略 (`GET /beta/trustFramework/policies`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-2409">_Policy.Read.All_: Read your organization's trust framework policies (`GET /beta/trustFramework/policies`)</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-2410">_Policy.Read.All_ 读取你所在组织的功能推出策略 (`GET /beta/directory/featureRolloutPolicies`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-2410">_Policy.Read.All_: Read your organization's feature rollout policies (`GET /beta/directory/featureRolloutPolicies`)</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-2411">_Policy.ReadWrite.AccessReview_：读取和写入组织的访问评审策略 (`PATCH /beta/policies/accessReviewPolicy`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-2411">_Policy.ReadWrite.AccessReview_: Read and write your organization's access review policies (`PATCH /beta/policies/accessReviewPolicy`)</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-2412">_Policy.ReadWrite.ApplicationConfiguration_：读取和写入组织的应用程序配置策略 (`POST /beta/policies/tokenLifetimePolicies`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-2412">_Policy.ReadWrite.ApplicationConfiguration_: Read and write your organization's application configuration policies (`POST /beta/policies/tokenLifetimePolicies`)</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-2413">_Policy.ReadWrite.AuthenticationFlows_：读取和写入你组织的身份验证流策略 (`PATCH /beta/policies/authenticationFlowsPolicy`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-2413">_Policy.ReadWrite.AuthenticationFlows_: Read and write your organization's authentication flows policy (`PATCH /beta/policies/authenticationFlowsPolicy`)</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-2414">_Policy.ReadWrite.ConditionalAccess_：读取和写入你组织的条件访问策略 (`POST /beta/identity/conditionalAccess/policies`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-2414">_Policy.ReadWrite.ConditionalAccess_: Read and write your organization's conditional access policies (`POST /beta/identity/conditionalAccess/policies`)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-2470">对于通过委派权限读取程序和程序控件的应用，登录的用户必须是以下管理员角色之一的成员：全局管理员、安全管理员、安全读取者或用户管理员。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-2470">For an app with delegated permissions to read programs and program controls, the signed-in user must be a member of one of the following administrator roles: Global Administrator, Security Administrator, Security Reader or User Administrator.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-2471">对于通过委派权限写入程序和程序控件的应用，登录的用户必须是以下管理员角色之一的成员：全局管理员、安全管理员、安全读取者或用户管理员。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-2471">For an app with delegated permissions to write programs and program controls, the signed-in user must be a member of one of the following administrator roles: Global Administrator or User Administrator.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-2472">若要详细了解管理员角色，请参阅[在 Azure Active Directory 中分配管理员角色](/azure/active-directory/active-directory-assign-admin-roles)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-2472">For more information about administrator roles, see [Assigning administrator roles in Azure Active Directory](/azure/active-directory/active-directory-assign-admin-roles).</span></span>

### <a name="remarks"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ca75-2551">说明</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-2551">Remarks</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-2552">使用 _RoleManagement.Read.Directory_ 权限，应用程序可以读取 directoryRoles 和 directoryRoleTemplates。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-2552">With the _RoleManagement.Read.Directory_ permission an application can read directoryRoles and directoryRoleTemplates.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-2553">这包括读取目录角色的成员身份信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-2553">This includes reading membership information for directory roles.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-2554">使用 _RoleManagement.ReadWrite.Directory_ 权限，应用程序可以读取和写入 directoryRoles（directoryRoleTemplates 是只读资源）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-2554">With the _RoleManagement.ReadWrite.Directory_ permission an application can read and write directoryRoles (directoryRoleTemplates are readonly resources).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-2555">这包括向目录角色添加成员和从目录角色中删除成员。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-2555">This includes adding and removing members to and from directory roles.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-2556">角色管理权限仅对工作或学校帐户有效。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-2556">Role management permissions are only valid for work or school accounts.</span></span>

### <a name="example-usage"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ca75-2557">用法示例</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-2557">Example usage</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-2558">_RoleManagement.Read.Directory_：读取可用角色模板列表 (`GET /directoryRoleTemplates`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-2558">_RoleManagement.Read.Directory_: Read the list of available role templates (`GET /directoryRoleTemplates`)</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-2559">_RoleManagement.Read.Directory_：读取你的目录中已激活角色的列表 (`GET /directoryRoles`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-2559">_RoleManagement.Read.Directory_: Read the list of activated roles in your directory (`GET /directoryRoles`)</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-2560">_RoleManagement.Read.Directory_：读取某一角色的成员列表 (`GET /directoryRoles/<id>/members`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-2560">_RoleManagement.Read.Directory_: Read the list of members for a role (`GET /directoryRoles/<id>/members`)</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-2561">_RoleManagement.Read.Directory_：读取某一角色的管理单元范围的成员列表 (`GET /directoryRoles/<id>/scopedMembers`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-2561">_RoleManagement.Read.Directory_: Read the list of administrative unit-scoped members for a role (`GET /directoryRoles/<id>/scopedMembers`)</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-2562">_RoleManagement.ReadWrite.Directory_：激活来自角色模板的目录角色 (`POST /directoryRoles`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-2562">_RoleManagement.ReadWrite.Directory_: Activate a directory role from a role template  (`POST /directoryRoles`)</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-2563">_RoleManagement.ReadWrite.Directory_：将成员添加到目录角色 (`POST /directoryRoles/<id>/members`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-2563">_RoleManagement.ReadWrite.Directory_: Add a member to a directory role (`POST /directoryRoles/<id>/members`)</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-2564">_RoleManagement.ReadWrite.Directory_：将管理单元范围的成员添加到目录角色 (`POST /directoryRoles/<id>/scopedMembers`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-2564">_RoleManagement.ReadWrite.Directory_: Add an administrative unit-scoped member to a directory role (`POST /directoryRoles/<id>/scopedMembers`)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-2565">有关涉及多个权限的更复杂的情况，请参阅[权限方案](#permission-scenarios)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-2565">For more complex scenarios involving multiple permissions, see [Permission scenarios](#permission-scenarios).</span></span>

## <a name="search-permissions"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ca75-2609">搜索权限</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-2609">Search permissions</span></span>

### <a name="remarks"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ca75-2632">注解</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-2632">Remarks</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-2633">搜索权限仅对工作或学校帐户有效。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-2633">Search permissions are only valid for work or school accounts.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-2634">此搜索权限仅适用于通过索引 API 引入的数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-2634">This search permission is only applicable to ingested data from the indexing API.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-2635">通过搜索访问数据需要对项目具有读取权限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-2635">Access to data via search requires the read permission to the item.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-2636">示例：_Files.Read.All_ 用于通过搜索访问文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-2636">Ex : _Files.Read.All_ to access files via search.</span></span>

#### <a name="delegated"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ca75-2638">委派</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-2638">Delegated</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-2639">_ExternalItem.Read.All_：通过 [搜索 API](/graph/api/resources/search-api-overview) (`POST /search/query`) 访问外部数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-2639">_ExternalItem.Read.All_ :  Access external data from the [search API](/graph/api/resources/search-api-overview) (`POST /search/query`).</span></span>

### <a name="example-usage"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ca75-2711">用法示例</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-2711">Example usage</span></span>

#### <a name="delegated-and-application"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ca75-2712">委派和应用程序</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-2712">Delegated and Application</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-2713">_SecurityEvents.Read.All_：从对租户可用的所有许可安全提供程序中读取所有安全警报的列表 (`GET /beta/security/alerts`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-2713">_SecurityEvents.Read.All_: Read the list of all security alerts from all licensed security providers available to your tenant (`GET /beta/security/alerts`)</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-2714">_SecurityEvents.ReadWrite.All_：更新或读取对租户可用的所有许可安全提供程序中的安全警报 (`PATCH /beta/security/alerts/{id}`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-2714">_SecurityEvents.ReadWrite.All_: Update or read security alerts from all licensed security providers available to your tenant  (`PATCH /beta/security/alerts/{id}`)</span></span>

### <a name="remarks"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ca75-2798">注解</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-2798">Remarks</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-2799">站点权限仅对工作或学校帐户有效。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-2799">Sites permissions are valid only on work or school accounts.</span></span>

### <a name="example-usage"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ca75-2800">用法示例</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-2800">Example usage</span></span>

#### <a name="delegated"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ca75-2801">委派</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-2801">Delegated</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-2802">_Sites.Read.All_：读取 SharePoint 根网站上的列表 (`GET /v1.0/sites/root/lists`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-2802">_Sites.Read.All_: Read the lists on the SharePoint root site (`GET /v1.0/sites/root/lists`)</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-2803">_Sites.ReadWrite.All_：在 SharePoint 列表中新建列表项 (`POST /v1.0/sites/root/lists/123/items`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-2803">_Sites.ReadWrite.All_: Create new list items in a SharePoint list (`POST /v1.0/sites/root/lists/123/items`)</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-2804">_Sites.Manage.All_：将新列表添加到 SharePoint 网站 (`POST /v1.0/sites/root/lists`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-2804">_Sites.Manage.All_: Add a new list to a SharePoint site (`POST /v1.0/sites/root/lists`)</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-2805">_Sites.FullControl.All_：对 SharePoint 网站和列表的完全访问权限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-2805">_Sites.FullControl.All_: Complete access to SharePoint sites and lists.</span></span>

---

| <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-2829">_Tasks.ReadWrite.Shared_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-2829">_Tasks.ReadWrite.Shared_</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-2830">读取和写入用户任务和共享任务（预览版）</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-2830">Read and write user and shared tasks (preview)</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-2831">允许应用创建、读取、更新和删除用户有权访问的任务，包括用户个人任务和共享任务。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-2831">Allows the app to create, read, update, and delete tasks a user has permissions to, including their own and shared tasks.</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-2832">否</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-2832">No</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-2833">否</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-2833">No</span></span> |

#### <a name="application-permissions"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ca75-2834">应用程序权限</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-2834">Application permissions</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-2835">无。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-2835">None.</span></span>

### <a name="remarks"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ca75-2836">说明</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-2836">Remarks</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-2837">_任务_ 权限用于控制对微软待办任务和 Outlook 任务的访问权限（已弃用）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-2837">_Tasks_ permissions are used to control access for To Do tasks and Outlook tasks(deprecated).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-2838">Microsoft Planner 任务的访问权限由 [_组_ 权限](#group-permissions)控制。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-2838">Access for Microsoft Planner tasks is controlled by [_Group_ permissions](#group-permissions).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-p229">目前仅工作或学校帐户支持 _共享_ 权限。即使具有 _共享_ 权限，如果未授予拥有共享内容的用户在文件夹内修改内容访问用户权限，读取和写入仍会失败。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-p229">_Shared_ permissions are currently only supported for work or school accounts. Even with _Shared_ permissions, reads and writes may fail if the user who owns the shared content has not granted the accessing user permissions to modify content within the folder.</span></span>

### <a name="example-usage"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ca75-2841">用法示例</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-2841">Example usage</span></span>
#### <a name="delegated"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ca75-2842">委派</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-2842">Delegated</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-2843">_Tasks.Read_：获取用户邮箱中的所有任务 (`GET /me/outlook/tasks`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-2843">_Tasks.Read_: Get all tasks in a user's mailbox (`GET /me/outlook/tasks`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-2844">_Tasks.Read.Shared_：在文件夹中访问组织中其他用户与你共享的任务 (`Get /users{id|userPrincipalName}/outlook/taskfolders/{id}/tasks`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-2844">_Tasks.Read.Shared_: Access tasks in a folder shared to you by another user in your organization (`Get /users{id|userPrincipalName}/outlook/taskfolders/{id}/tasks`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-2845">_Tasks.ReadWrite_：将事件添加到用户的默认任务文件夹 (`POST /me/outlook/tasks`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-2845">_Tasks.ReadWrite_: Add an event to the user's default task folder (`POST /me/outlook/tasks`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-2846">_Tasks.Read_：获取用户邮箱中的所有未完成任务 (`GET /users/{id | userPrincipalName}/outlook/tasks?$filter=status ne 'completed'`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-2846">_Tasks.Read_: Get all uncompleted tasks in a user's mailbox (`GET /users/{id | userPrincipalName}/outlook/tasks?$filter=status ne 'completed'`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-2847">_Tasks.ReadWrite_：更新用户邮箱中的任务 (`PATCH /users/{id | userPrincipalName}/outlook/tasks/id`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-2847">_Tasks.ReadWrite_: Update a task in a user's mailbox (`PATCH /users/{id | userPrincipalName}/outlook/tasks/id`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-2848">_Tasks.ReadWrite.Shared_：代表其他用户完成任务 (`POST /users/{id | userPrincipalName}/outlook/tasks/id/complete`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-2848">_Tasks.ReadWrite.Shared_: Complete a task on behalf of another user (`POST /users/{id | userPrincipalName}/outlook/tasks/id/complete`).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-2849">有关涉及多个权限的更复杂的情况，请参阅[权限方案](#permission-scenarios)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-2849">For more complex scenarios involving multiple permissions, see [Permission scenarios](#permission-scenarios).</span></span>

### <a name="remarks"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ca75-3333">注解</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-3333">Remarks</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-3334">上述所有权限仅对工作或学校帐户有效。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-3334">All the permissions above are valid only for work or school accounts.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-3335">若要使应用能够阅读或编写委派权限的所有协议或协议接受情况，登录用户必须分配有全局管理员、条件访问管理员或安全管理员角色。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-3335">For an app to read or write all agreements or agreement acceptances with delegated permissions, the signed-in user must be assigned the Global Administrator, Conditional Access Administrator or Security Administrator role.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-3336">若要详细了解管理员角色，请参阅[在 Azure Active Directory 中分配管理员角色](/azure/active-directory/active-directory-assign-admin-roles)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-3336">For more information about administrator roles, see [Assigning administrator roles in Azure Active Directory](/azure/active-directory/active-directory-assign-admin-roles).</span></span>

### <a name="example-usage"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ca75-3337">用法示例</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-3337">Example usage</span></span>

#### <a name="delegated"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ca75-3338">委派</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-3338">Delegated</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-3339">以下使用对两种委派权限均有效：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-3339">The following usages are valid for both delegated permissions:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-3340">_Agreement.Read.All_：阅读所有使用条款协议 (`GET /beta/agreements`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-3340">_Agreement.Read.All_: Read all terms of use agreements (`GET /beta/agreements`)</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-3341">_Agreement.ReadWrite.All_：阅读和编写所有使用条款协议 (`POST /beta/agreements`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-3341">_Agreement.ReadWrite.All_: Read and write all terms of use agreements (`POST /beta/agreements`)</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-3342">_AgreementAcceptance.Read_：阅读用户使用条款接受状态 (`GET /beta/me/agreementAcceptances`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-3342">_AgreementAcceptance.Read_ Read user terms of use acceptance statuses (`GET /beta/me/agreementAcceptances`)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-3343">有关涉及多个权限的更复杂的情况，请参阅[权限方案](#permission-scenarios)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-3343">For more complex scenarios involving multiple permissions, see [Permission scenarios](#permission-scenarios).</span></span>

### <a name="remarks"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ca75-3601">注解</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-3601">Remarks</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-3602">若要使用通用打印服务，用户或应用的租户除了前面列出的权限外，还必须具有有效的通用打印订阅。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-3602">To use the Universal Print service, the user or app's tenant must have an active Universal Print subscription in addition to the  permissions listed earlier.</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-3603">某些权限可区分打印作业元数据和有效负载。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-3603">Some permissions distinguish between print job metadata and payload.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-3604">元数据描述了打印作业的配置（其名称和文档配置，例如应该装订还是彩色打印）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-3604">Metadata describes the configuration of a print job (its name and document configuration, such as whether it should be stapled or printed in color).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-3605">有效负载是文档数据本身（要打印的 PDF 或 XPS 文件。）</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-3605">Payload is the document data itself (the PDF or XPS file to be printed.)</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-3606">所有 PrintJob.\* 权限还至少需要 Printer.Read.All（或更多特权权限），因为打印作业存储在打印机中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-3606">All PrintJob.\* permissions also require at least Printer.Read.All (or a more prviliged permission) because print jobs are stored within printers.</span></span>

### <a name="example-usage"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ca75-3607">用法示例</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-3607">Example usage</span></span>

#### <a name="delegated"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ca75-3608">Delegated</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-3608">Delegated</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-3609">_Printer.Read.All_：获取租户中所有打印机的列表 (`GET /print/printers`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-3609">_Printer.Read.All_: Get a list of all printers in the tenant (`GET /print/printers`)</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-3610">_PrintJob.Read.All_：获取排队到打印机的所有打印作业的列表 (`GET /print/printers/{id}/jobs`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-3610">_PrintJob.Read.All_: Get a list of all print jobs queued to a Printer (`GET /print/printers/{id}/jobs`)</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-3611">_Printer.FullControl.All_：删除（注销）打印机 (`DELETE /print/printers/{id}`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-3611">_Printer.FullControl.All_: Delete (unregister) a printer (`DELETE /print/printers/{id}`)</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-3612">_PrintJob.ReadWriteBasic.All_：更新打印作业的元数据（例如当前状态）(`PATCH /print/printers/{id}/jobs/{id}`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-3612">_PrintJob.ReadWriteBasic.All_: Update metadata (such as current status) of print jobs (`PATCH /print/printers/{id}/jobs/{id}`)</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-3613">_PrintJob.ReadWrite.All_：创建打印作业并向其上传文档数据 (`POST /print/printers/{id}/jobs`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-3613">_PrintJob.ReadWrite.All_: Create print jobs and upload document data to them (`POST /print/printers/{id}/jobs`)</span></span>

#### <a name="application"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ca75-3614">应用程序</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-3614">Application</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-3615">_Printer.Read.All_：获取租户中所有打印机的列表 (`GET /print/printers`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-3615">_Printer.Read.All_: Get a list of all printers in the tenant (`GET /print/printers`)</span></span>
