| <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-3688">_User.Export.All_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-3688">_User.Export.All_</span></span>       |    <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-3689">导出用户数据</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-3689">Export users' data</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-3690">允许应用导出组织用户数据，而无需是登录用户。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-3690">Allows the app to export organizational users' data, without a signed-in user.</span></span>| <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-3691">是</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-3691">Yes</span></span> |
| <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-3692">_User.ManageIdentities.All_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-3692">_User.ManageIdentities.All_</span></span>       |    <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-3693">管理所有用户标识</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-3693">Manage all user identities</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-p280">允许应用程序在没有登录用户的情况下读取、更新和删除与用户帐户相关联的标识。这控制了用户可以使用哪些标识进行登录。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-p280">Allows an application to read, update and delete identities that are associated with a user's account, without a signed in user. This controls which identities users can sign-in with.</span></span> |  <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-3696">是</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-3696">Yes</span></span> |

### <a name="remarks"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ca75-3697">说明</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-3697">Remarks</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-p281">通过 _User.Read_ 权限，应用还可以通过 [organization](/graph/api/resources/organization) 资源读取工作或学校帐户的已登录用户的基本公司信息。以下属性可用：ID、displayName 和 verifiedDomains。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-p281">With the _User.Read_ permission, an app can also read the basic company information of the signed-in user for a work or school account through the [organization](/graph/api/resources/organization) resource. The following properties are available: id, displayName, and verifiedDomains.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-p282">对于工作或学校帐户，完整个人资料包括 [User](/graph/api/resources/user) 资源的所有声明属性。在读取时，默认情况下仅返回有限数量的属性。若要读取不在默认设置中的属性，请使用 `$select`。默认属性包括：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-p282">For work or school accounts, the full profile includes all of the declared properties of the [User](/graph/api/resources/user) resource. On reads, only a limited number of properties are returned by default. To read properties that are not in the default set, use `$select`. The default properties are:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-3704">displayName</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-3704">displayName</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-3705">givenName</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-3705">givenName</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-3706">jobTitle</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-3706">jobTitle</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-3707">mail</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-3707">mail</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-3708">mobilePhone</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-3708">mobilePhone</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-3709">officeLocation</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-3709">officeLocation</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-3710">preferredLanguage</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-3710">preferredLanguage</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-3711">surname</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-3711">surname</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-3712">userPrincipalName</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-3712">userPrincipalName</span></span>

 <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-3713">_User.ReadWrite_ 和 _User.Readwrite.All_ 委派权限允许应用更新工作或学校帐户的以下配置文件属性：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-3713">_User.ReadWrite_ and _User.Readwrite.All_ delegated permissions allow the app to update the following profile properties for work or school accounts:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-3714">aboutMe</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-3714">aboutMe</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-3715">birthday</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-3715">birthday</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-3716">hireDate</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-3716">hireDate</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-3717">interests</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-3717">interests</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-3718">mobilePhone</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-3718">mobilePhone</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-3719">mySite</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-3719">mySite</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-3720">pastProjects</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-3720">pastProjects</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-3721">photo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-3721">photo</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-3722">preferredName</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-3722">preferredName</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-3723">responsibilities</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-3723">responsibilities</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-3724">schools</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-3724">schools</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-3725">skills</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-3725">skills</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-3726">通过 _User.ReadWrite.All_ 应用程序权限，应用可更新工作或学校帐户的所有声明属性，但密码除外。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-3726">With the _User.ReadWrite.All_ application permission, the app can update all of the declared properties of work or school accounts except for password.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-3727">在具有 _User.ReadWrite.All_ 委托或应用程序权限的情况下，如需更新其他用户的 **businessPhones**、**mobilePhone** 或 **otherMails**，仅允许针对非管理员或分配了以下角色之一的用户执行该操作：目录读取者、来宾邀请者、消息中心读取者和报告读取者。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-3727">With the _User.ReadWrite.All_ delegated or application permission, updating another user's **businessPhones**, **mobilePhone** or **otherMails** is only allowed on users who are non-administrators or assigned one of the following roles: Directory Readers, Guest Inviter, Message Center Reader and Reports Reader.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-3728">有关详细信息，请参阅 [Azure AD 可用角色](/azure/active-directory/users-groups-roles/directory-assign-admin-roles#available-roles)中的支持人员（密码）管理员。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-3728">For more details, see Helpdesk (Password) Administrator in [Azure AD available roles](/azure/active-directory/users-groups-roles/directory-assign-admin-roles#available-roles).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-3729">要读取或写入工作或学校帐户的直接下属 (`directReports`) 或经理 (`manager`)，应用必须具有 _User.Read.All_（只读）或 _User.ReadWrite.All_。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-3729">To read or write direct reports (`directReports`) or the manager (`manager`) of a work or school account, the app must have either _User.Read.All_ (read only) or _User.ReadWrite.All_.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-p284">_User.ReadBasic.All_ 权限限制应用访问称为基本个人资料的有限属性集。这是因为完整的个人资料可能包含敏感的目录信息。基本个人资料仅包括以下属性：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-p284">The _User.ReadBasic.All_ permission constrains app access to a limited set of properties known as the basic profile. This is because the full profile might contain sensitive directory information. The basic profile includes only the following properties:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-3733">displayName</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-3733">displayName</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-3734">givenName</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-3734">givenName</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-3735">mail</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-3735">mail</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-3736">photo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-3736">photo</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-3737">surname</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-3737">surname</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-3738">userPrincipalName</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-3738">userPrincipalName</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-p285">若要读取用户的组成员资格 (`memberOf`)，则应用必须具有 [_Group.Read.All_](#group-permissions) 或 [_Group.ReadWrite.All_](#group-permissions)。但是，如果用户还具有 [directoryRole](/graph/api/resources/directoryrole) 或 [administrativeUnit](/graph/api/resources/administrativeunit?view=graph-rest-beta&preserve-view=true) 中的成员资格，则应用还将需要有效权限来读取这些资源，否则 Microsoft Graph 将返回错误。这意味着应用还需要 [目录权限](#directory-permissions)，而对于委派权限来说，已登录的用户还需要组织内的足够特权来访问目录角色和管理单元。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-p285">To read the group memberships of a user (`memberOf`), the app must have either [_Group.Read.All_](#group-permissions) or [_Group.ReadWrite.All_](#group-permissions). However, if the user also has membership in a [directoryRole](/graph/api/resources/directoryrole) or an [administrativeUnit](/graph/api/resources/administrativeunit?view=graph-rest-beta&preserve-view=true), the app will need effective permissions to read those resources too, or Microsoft Graph will return an error. This means the app will also need [Directory permissions](#directory-permissions), and, for delegated permissions, the signed-in user will also need sufficient privileges in the organization to access directory roles and administrative units.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-3742">使用 _User.ManageIdentities.All_ 委派权限或应用程序权限，可以更新用户标识 (`identities`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-3742">With the _User.ManageIdentities.All_ delegated or application permission, it is possible to update the identities (`identities`) of a user.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-3743">这包括具有基于电子邮件地址或姓名的登录名的联合标识（亦称为“社交标识”）或本地标识。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-3743">This includes federated (or social identities) or local identities with email or name-based sign-in names.</span></span>

### <a name="example-usage"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ca75-3744">用法示例</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-3744">Example usage</span></span>

#### <a name="delegated"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ca75-3745">委派</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-3745">Delegated</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-3746">_User.Read_：读取登录用户的完整配置文件 (`GET /me`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-3746">_User.Read_: Read the full profile for the signed-in user (`GET /me`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-3747">_User.ReadWrite_：更新登录用户的照片 (`PUT /me/photo/$value`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-3747">_User.ReadWrite_: Update the photo of the signed-in user (`PUT /me/photo/$value`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-3748">_User.ReadBasic.All_：查找名称以“David”开头的所有用户 (`GET /users?$filter=startswith(displayName,'David')`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-3748">_User.ReadBasic.All_: Find all users whose name starts with "David" (`GET /users?$filter=startswith(displayName,'David')`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-3749">_User.Read.All_：读取用户的经理 (`GET /users/{id | userPrincipalName}/manager`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-3749">_User.Read.All_: Read a user's manager (`GET /users/{id | userPrincipalName}/manager`).</span></span>

#### <a name="application"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ca75-3750">应用程序</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-3750">Application</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-3751">_User.Read.All_：通过 delta 查询读取所有用户和关系 (`GET /beta/users/delta?$select=displayName,givenName,surname`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-3751">_User.Read.All_: Read all users and relationships through delta query (`GET /beta/users/delta?$select=displayName,givenName,surname`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-3752">_User.ReadWrite.All_：更新组织中任意用户的照片 (`PUT /users/{id | userPrincipalName}/photo/$value`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-3752">_User.ReadWrite.All_: Update the photo for any user in the organization (`PUT /users/{id | userPrincipalName}/photo/$value`).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-3753">有关涉及多个权限的更复杂的情况，请参阅[权限方案](#permission-scenarios)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-3753">For more complex scenarios involving multiple permissions, see [Permission scenarios](#permission-scenarios).</span></span>

### <a name="remarks"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ca75-3768">说明</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-3768">Remarks</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-3769">*UserActivity.ReadWrite.CreatedByApp* 对 Microsoft 帐户和工作或学校帐户均有效。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-3769">*UserActivity.ReadWrite.CreatedByApp* is valid for both Microsoft accounts and work or school accounts.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-3770">与此权限相关联的 *CreatedByApp* 约束指示服务将基于调用应用的标识（MSA 应用 ID 或针对跨平台应用程序标识配置的一组应用 ID）对结果应用隐式筛选。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-3770">The *CreatedByApp* constraint associated with this permission indicates the service will apply implicit filtering to results based on the identity of the calling app, either the MSA app id or a set of app ids configured for a cross-platform application identity.</span></span>

### <a name="example-usage"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ca75-3771">用法示例</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-3771">Example usage</span></span>

#### <a name="delegated"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ca75-3772">委派</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-3772">Delegated</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-3773">_UserActivity.ReadWrite.CreatedByApp_：基于最后一天发布的相关联的历史记录项来获取最近特定用户活动的列表。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-3773">_UserActivity.ReadWrite.CreatedByApp_: Get a list of recent unique user activities based on associated history items published in the last day.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-3774">(GET /me/activities/recent)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-3774">(GET /me/activities/recent).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-3775">_UserActivity.ReadWrite.CreatedByApp_：发布或更新可能由应用程序用户恢复的用户活动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-3775">_UserActivity.ReadWrite.CreatedByApp_: Publish or update a user activity which may be resumed by the user of the application.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-3776">(PUT /me/activities/%2Farticle%3F12345)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-3776">(PUT /me/activities/%2Farticle%3F12345).</span></span>
*   <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-3777">_UserActivity.ReadWrite.CreatedByApp_：发布或更新指定用户活动的历史记录项，以表示用户参与的时间段。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-3777">_UserActivity.ReadWrite.CreatedByApp_: Publish or update a history item for a specified user activity in order to represent the period of user engagement.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-3778">(PUT /me/activities/{id}/historyItems/{id})。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-3778">(PUT /me/activities/{id}/historyItems/{id}).</span></span>
*   <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-3779">_UserActivity.ReadWrite.CreatedByApp_：根据用户发起的请求删除用户活动或删除无效数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-3779">_UserActivity.ReadWrite.CreatedByApp_: Delete a user activity in response to user initiated request or to remove invalid data.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-3780">(DELETE /me/activities/{id})。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-3780">(DELETE /me/activities/{id}).</span></span>
*   <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-3781">_UserActivity.ReadWrite.CreatedByApp_：根据用户发起的请求删除历史记录项或删除无效数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-3781">_UserActivity.ReadWrite.CreatedByApp_: Delete a history item in response to user initiated request or to remove invalid data.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-3782">(DELETE /me/activities/{id}/historyItems/{id})。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-3782">(DELETE /me/activities/{id}/historyItems/{id}).</span></span>

## <a name="user-authentication-method-permissions-preview"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ca75-3783">用户身份验证方法权限（[预览版](#permissions-availability-status)）</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-3783">User authentication method permissions ([preview](#permissions-availability-status))</span></span>

#### <a name="delegated-permissions"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ca75-3784">委派权限</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-3784">Delegated permissions</span></span>

### <a name="remarks"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ca75-3833">备注</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-3833">Remarks</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-p298">用户身份验证方法权限用于管理用户的身份验证方法。借助这些权限，委派的用户或应用程序可以注册用户的新身份验证方法，读取用户已注册的身份验证方法，更新这些身份验证方法，以及从用户中删除它们。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-p298">User authentication method permissions are used to manage authentication methods on users. With these permissions, a delegated user or application can register new authentication methods on a user, read the authentication methods the user already has registered, update those authentication methods, and remove them from the user.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-p299">借助这些权限，可以读取和管理用户的所有身份验证方法。这包括用于以下方面的方法：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-p299">With these permissions, all authentication methods can be read and managed on a user. This includes methods used for:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-3838">主要身份验证（密码）</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-3838">Primary authentication (password)</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-3839">多重身份验证/MFA（电话号码）的第二因素</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-3839">Second factor of multi-factor authentication/MFA (phone numbers)</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-3840">自助密码重置/SSPR（电子邮件地址）</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-3840">Self-Service Password Reset/SSPR (email address)</span></span>

### <a name="remarks"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ca75-3862">注解</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-3862">Remarks</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-3863">上述所有权限仅对工作或学校帐户有效。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-3863">All the permissions above are valid only for work or school accounts.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-3864">登录用户必须分配有全局管理员或 Intune 管理员角色，应用才能使用委派权限读取或写入所有 Windows 更新部署设置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-3864">For an app to read or write all Windows update deployment settings with delegated permissions, the signed-in user must be assigned the Global Administrator or Intune Administrator role.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ca75-3865">若要详细了解管理员角色，请参阅[在 Azure Active Directory 中分配管理员角色](/azure/active-directory/active-directory-assign-admin-roles)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-3865">For more information about administrator roles, see [Assigning administrator roles in Azure Active Directory](/azure/active-directory/active-directory-assign-admin-roles).</span></span>

|<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-3889">_Policy.ReadWrite.AuthenticationMethod_（个人预览版）</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-3889">_Policy.ReadWrite.AuthenticationMethod_ (private preview)</span></span>   |<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-3890">读取和写入所有身份验证方法策略。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-3890">Read and write all authentication methods policies.</span></span>    |<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-3891">允许应用读取和写入 Azure AD 租户上的所有身份验证方法策略。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-3891">Allows the app to read and write all authentication methods policies on an Azure AD tenant.</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-3892">是</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-3892">Yes</span></span>|


### <a name="remarks"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ca75-3893">备注</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-3893">Remarks</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-3894">身份验证方法策略权限用于管理身份验证方法策略中的设置，包括启用和禁用身份验证方法、允许用户和组使用这些方法以及配置与用户可以在租户中注册和使用的身份验证方法相关的其他设置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-3894">Authentication methods policy permissions are used to manage settings in the authentication methods policy, including enabling and disabling authentication methods, allowing users and groups to use those methods, and configuring other settings related to the authentication methods that users may register and use in a tenant.</span></span>

## <a name="permission-scenarios"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ca75-3895">权限方案</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-3895">Permission scenarios</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ca75-p302">本节介绍一些面向组织中 [user](/graph/api/resources/user) 和 [group](/graph/api/resources/group) 资源的常见方案。这些表显示了应用执行方案要求的特定操作所需的权限。请注意，在某些情况下，应用执行特定操作的能力取决于权限是应用程序权限还是委派权限。如果是委派权限，应用的有效权限还将取决于组织内已登录用户的特权。有关详细信息，请参阅[委派权限、应用程序权限和有效权限](auth/auth-concepts.md#microsoft-graph-permissions)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ca75-p302">This section shows some common scenarios that target [user](/graph/api/resources/user) and [group](/graph/api/resources/group) resources in an organization. The tables show the permissions that an app needs to be able to perform specific operations required by the scenario. Note that in some cases the ability of the app to perform specific operations will depend on whether a permission is an application or delegated permission. In the case of delegated permissions, the app's effective permissions will also depend on the privileges of the signed-in user within the organization. For more information, see  [Delegated permissions, Application permissions, and effective permissions](auth/auth-concepts.md#microsoft-graph-permissions).</span></span>
